Germany's Gold Reserves Continue to Decline, Financial Circles Express Concern 43

(Berlin) The German Reichsbank has again reduced its gold reserves by 25 million marks. Thus, Germany's gold coverage now stands at 4.8%. The continued decline in Germany's gold reserves has financial circles expressing concern today, believing that the German Reichsbank will eventually rely solely on securities as coverage. As of May 15th, securities were worth a total of 319 million marks. A year ago, Germany's gold coverage was 8.5%. In addition, banknote issuance has increased by 124 million marks. (17th Reuters Dispatch)

China Purchases Vehicles for the Yuehan Railway from Britain and a Ferry for Pukou 44

(London) The Chinese Purchasing Commission is now soliciting bids for the supply of goods wagons and passenger carriages for the Yuehan Railway, including fourteen powerful engines, two open-car engines, and one hundred and seventy 40-ton steel wagons, as well as four large engines and four smaller engines for the Jiaoji Railway, and a train ferry for Pukou. The entire batch of supplies is worth approximately £250,000. (17th Reuters Dispatch)

The Disarmament Conference Is Nearing Its End: The Great Powers Are Competing to Expand Their Armaments, and Two Years of Painstaking Effort Are Ending in This Way 45

Various parties still do not admit failure.

French Foreign Minister Efforts to refute rumors are great.

Britain plans to make a final effort to facilitate a partial agreement.

Washington prepares to issue a statement clarifying its attitude on disarmament.

(Geneva) According to recent developments today, the Disarmament Conference, which European politicians have painstakingly worked on for two years, has indeed come to an end. When the General Commission of the Disarmament Conference meets on May 29, this matter will be formally announced. This decision is reportedly the result of talks between diplomats from Britain, France, Italy, and the United States. The four diplomats are now devising a way to conclude the conference for approval by the General Commission of Disarmament. The Associated Press was the first to disclose the news of the dissolution of the Disarmament Conference, which was repeatedly denied by European politicians involved in the matter. However, representatives from various countries subsequently admitted that the General Commission of Disarmament may take this step. Britain has always advocated the conclusion of a disarmament treaty, but it is now clear that general disarmament is hopeless. However, some British politicians still believe that it is not impossible to conclude an air force disarmament agreement. It is said that American diplomats participated in the discussions on dissolving the Disarmament Conference, but they only acted behind the scenes. Military experts here are now eager for the White House to issue a statement on the US's disarmament policy. The White House announced last night that President Roosevelt and the American disarmament representative Davis are preparing a joint statement to be released when Mr. Davis goes to Geneva to attend the General Commission of Disarmament on May 29. (17th National Telegram)

(Geneva) The League of Nations quickly denied reports today that the Disarmament Conference had decided to adjourn. French Foreign Minister Barthou refuted it with particular vehemence, saying that he still has hope for the Disarmament Conference. However, despite this denial from the League of Nations, it is generally recognized that the conference is unlikely to succeed. Therefore, the possibility of the General Commission of Disarmament reporting back to the League of Nations Executive Council has become a topic of discussion. Reliable sources believe that when the General Commission meets on May 29, it may not be easy to extend the life of the Disarmament Conference beyond half a month. Many people firmly believe that the best and most prudent approach is to have a long adjournment, during which economic conditions may create better opportunities to resolve disarmament. At the same time, a telegram from Washington stated that President Roosevelt announced that he is preparing a document that fully clarifies the US's attitude toward disarmament, which will be announced by the American representative Davis, who is attending the Disarmament Conference in Geneva as an observer. However, President Roosevelt did not indicate any changes in US policy. (16th Reuters Dispatch) (London) London newspapers today expressed shock and dismay at the reports that the Disarmament Conference may collapse. The Archbishop of Canterbury issued a statement today on behalf of the Christian Church, saying that the failure of the Disarmament Conference would be an unforgivable betrayal of the public's expectations and aspirations. British Foreign Secretary Simon gave a speech here today, saying that he will go to Geneva to do his best to facilitate an agreement to resolve this complex and troubled situation. This statement by Simon suggests that although the hope for a large-scale convention has been extinguished, Britain is still determined to establish a framework convention to prohibit chemical and bacterial warfare, or to establish a European agreement to prohibit aerial attacks and abolish offensive weapons. The Huibao newspaper reported that Britain is now considering the details of an agreement to prohibit aerial bombardment, intending to obligate signatory countries to jointly bomb violators as a warning. If this effort by Britain still fails, the Disarmament Conference will hand this task back to the League of Nations, which will then transfer it to Germany, Russia, and the United States to handle. (17th Reuters Dispatch)

General Committee Convened at the End of the Month 46

(Geneva) The General Committee of the Disarmament Conference has now decided to convene on May 30. According to a bulletin issued by the League of Nations authorities this evening, the convening of this General Committee is being implemented by the Conference Chairman Henderson based on the resolution of the Steering Committee on April 10. (16th National Telegram)

(Geneva) The Presidium of the Disarmament Conference is scheduled to hold a closed meeting on May 28. (16th Havas Dispatch)

Rumors of Adjournment Reach Berlin, Causing a Moment of Surprise 47

(Berlin) The report from a foreign news agency here that the great powers have agreed in principle to an indefinite adjournment of the Disarmament Conference caused a sharp surprise here, but it soon subsided, as reports from London, Paris, and elsewhere immediately corrected it. According to reports from London, there has been no word of the Disarmament Conference closing, while reports from Paris directly call it inaccurate. German political circles feel that although the Disarmament Conference has reached a dead end, it will not readily admit its failure and hastily announce an adjournment until it finds a suitable way to shift responsibility. (16th National Telegram)

The Course of Disarmament Negotiations: Paris Publishes a Yellow Paper on Monday 48

(Geneva) French Foreign Minister Barthou gave a speech to representatives of the British and American press, saying that on April 6 of this year, France sent a verbal note to the British government on the issue of disarmament, explaining the guarantees for the implementation of the disarmament treaty. This verbal note will be published in the Yellow Paper on approximately Monday of next week. On January 29 of this year, Britain also sent a verbal note to the French government, proposing that France recognize Germany's partial rearmament, subject to supervision, in order to solve the disarmament problem by concluding a partial treaty on this basis. On March 17, France replied, "Although the British memorandum of January 29 has been modified and new implementation guarantees have been added as the basis for the treaty, France cannot accept it according to the current state of negotiations, because this approach leaves various unresolved technical and political problems unaddressed, which is too broad. If it is implemented, it will cause misunderstandings, because various technical and political problems have only been mentioned, but the raising of the issues cannot be regarded as a solution." The French verbal note of April 6, between March 17 (the French reply to the British memorandum of January 19) and April 17 (the French second formal reply to the British) is sufficient to prove that France still believes that disarmament can be solved even in the face of Germany's rearmament. After Barthou read out the French note, the reporters in attendance were reportedly moved. (16th Havas Dispatch)

The United States Implements a Large Naval Program: The First Batch of Ten Warships to Be Built, Requiring $40 Million US 49

(Washington) Navy Secretary Swanson announced today the construction of twelve destroyers, two destroyer leaders, and six submarines, totaling US$40 million. This project will commence immediately after the Public Works Administration allocates the funds and will become the first year's shipbuilding plan in the Vinson Naval Act. (16th National Telegram)

(Washington) According to Navy Secretary Swanson today, two destroyer squadron flagships, sixteen destroyers, and six submarines will be built immediately, and the funds can be allocated from the $132.2 million in emergency recovery program funds for the coming year requested by President Roosevelt. President Roosevelt's request to Congress includes $40 million for the construction of new ships, so that the strength of the US Navy reaches the level allowed by the London Naval Treaty, as well as $100 million for road construction, $48 million for the Tennessee Valley Authority development plan, and $35 million for public building. (16th Reuters Dispatch)

Japan's Competitive Shipbuilding Drives Financial Difficulties; Wakatsuki Expresses Concerns; Ministry of Communications Requests Huge Aviation Funds; Konoe Visits Army and Navy Ministers Before Departing for the US Yesterday 50

(Tokyo) Wakatsuki, the Japanese representative who participated in the London Naval Conference in 1930, stated today at a meeting of the Minseito party that the continuation of competitive warship construction will plunge Japan's finances into serious difficulties. He disagreed with the Finance Minister's proposal to make up the shortfall with borrowing. Wakatsuki advocated caution regarding increasing naval expenditures and did not oppose them. However, he said that it was contradictory to support a massive military buildup program while opposing tax increases to raise the necessary funds. (Reuters, 17th)

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of Communications' new budget for the next fiscal year places special emphasis on promoting aviation and maritime transport. It will request 1.8 million yuan for aviation expenses and 35 million yuan for shipping routes and shipbuilding subsidies. The details are as follows: (1) Aviation expenses between Taiwan and Fukuoka (10-year plan): 11 million yuan; (2) Aviation expenses between Tokyo and Sapporo (10-year plan): 5 million yuan; (3) Expansion costs for the Osaka airfield (2-year plan): 2 million yuan; (4) Shipbuilding subsidies (5-year plan): 25 million yuan; (5) Shipping route subsidies (5-year plan): 10 million yuan. (Hualian News Agency, 17th)

(Tokyo) Prince Fumimaro Konoe, President of the House of Peers, visited Army Minister Hayashi at his official residence at 2:00 PM yesterday. After a brief exchange of greetings regarding his trip to the US, they exchanged views on the current situation. He left at 3:30 PM. During the meeting, Minister Hayashi expressed the Army's views on the international situation for Prince Konoe's reference. Prince Konoe also visited the Navy Minister at 8:00 AM this morning and exchanged similar views. At 3:00 PM, he boarded the Asama Maru at Yokohama to depart for the US. (Dentsu News Agency, 17th)

(Tokyo) Navy Minister Osumi, with the consent of Prince Saionji's secretary, Harada Kumao, met with Prince Fumimaro Konoe, President of the House of Peers and goodwill envoy to the US, who is leaving for the US today. He explained in detail the Empire's attitude towards the next disarmament conference, namely: (1) advocating for changes to existing treaties, specifically differentiated ratios by warship type; (2) advocating for equality in the sense of national security, i.e., equality in armament rights. After the meeting, Navy Minister Osumi said, "Prince Konoe and I served together as attendants to Prince Saionji at the Paris Peace Conference, so our friendship is very close. Today's discussion covered disarmament issues and domestic and foreign political issues, etc. Taking advantage of his trip to the US, I conveyed my wishes in a lighthearted manner." (Dentsu News Agency, 17th)

Britain's New Defense Plan Places Special Emphasis on Air Defense Safety, Simultaneously Strengthening the Navy and Air Force 51

(London) The Daily Mail reported today that after Britain, France, Italy, and the United States agreed to an indefinite suspension of the disarmament conference, Britain is now planning a new and powerful defense plan. According to the newspaper's political reporter, the new defense plan will expand the Air Force to be on par with the world's strongest air forces. The expansion of the Navy is already being planned by the Admiralty, and other defense plans will also be implemented. Another reporter from the London Chronicle stated that the British government is still considering a disarmament treaty for the Air Force to salvage the remnants of the disarmament conference. The reporter continued, "Britain suggests that aerial bombardment of cities should be completely prohibited. Any country that violates this regulation should be immediately bombed by the other allied countries. Therefore, only if all countries accept Britain's air force disarmament proposal can Britain's large-scale air force expansion plan be cancelled." Air defense safety is a concern for Britain because London is the most vulnerable of the world's major cities to bombing. Daytime bombers within 300 miles and nighttime bombers within 600 miles can freely fly to London and drop bombs. The British Air Force only has 1,500 aircraft, which is insufficient for defense. Even in wartime, the British Air Force would only have 2,000 aircraft and 300,000 personnel. Therefore, in terms of first-line air power, Britain is almost on par with countries like Yugoslavia and Poland, far behind other major air powers. Moreover, the British Air Force is scattered throughout its territories, and only 480 first-line fighter aircraft are available to defend London. Furthermore, London's ground air defense equipment has been neglected. (National News Agency, 17th)

France Increases Defense Spending 53

(Paris) On February 28th of this year, the government submitted a bill to the Chamber of Deputies stipulating: (1) 1,115,000,000 francs will be allocated within the 1934-35 fiscal year to complete border defense works; (2) 980,000,000 francs will be allocated within 1934 to implement the aviation armament plan; (3) 825,000,000 francs will be used from 1934 to 1938 to build liquid fuel storage facilities, implement air defense measures, and strengthen the organization of seaplanes. This bill has been passed. Today, Finance Minister Germain-Martin, along with Army Minister Marshal Pétain, Air Inspector General General Denain, and Navy Minister Pietri, discussed this matter. As a result, it was decided that the Ministry of Finance would establish a special accounting system to manage these national defense engineering expenses.

Eden's Solemn Speech 57

(Geneva) The British government's Lord Privy Seal, Eden, proposed to the League of Nations Council today that all countries of the world unanimously embargo arms to Bolivia and Paraguay to stop the Gran Chaco war. When Eden put forward the proposal, he made a solemn speech, requesting the League of Nations Council to immediately telegraph the major countries of the world as well as the United States and the neighboring countries of Bolivia and Paraguay to implement a crackdown on the transportation of arms and military supplies to the two countries. Eden declared, "We should implement a stop to this unnecessary sacrifice of life. This is the responsibility of all the countries of the world as well as the neighboring countries of the belligerents. For the sake of peace, for the sake of humanity, we cannot hesitate any longer and should take urgent action." The attending representatives unanimously and enthusiastically supported this proposal. The Council can make a concrete decision tomorrow, but whether the arms embargo initiated by the League of Nations can be implemented depends on the attitude of the United States. As for the support of South American countries, there is no doubt. (National News Agency, 17th)

US Banking Faction and Roosevelt Reach Agreement on Silver Bill; President Will Send Special Message to Congress Within Days; Silver Price Set at US$1.29 62

(Washington) After months of contention between President Roosevelt and congressional silver advocates over the silver issue, a bill agreed upon by both sides has finally been reached. The White House issued a formal statement today stating that the President and silver advocates have reached an agreement, and the President will submit a special message to Congress within one or two days. It is understood that the message will propose improvements to the monetary system, and the legislation will be issued in a commanding style, with both approval and authorization elements. Silver-supporting senators are jubilant about the outcome of this White House meeting. Senator Pittman said that there is no misunderstanding on the silver bill issue, and the bill can be drafted immediately. According to reliable sources, the proposed silver bill will stipulate the following: (1) silver will be declared as currency in a commanding manner, and it will be stipulated that silver accounts for 25% of the reserves and gold accounts for 75%; (2) the Treasury Department will be authorized and directed to purchase silver until the price of silver reaches US$1.29 per ounce, or silver accounts for 25% of the total reserves; (3) the President will be authorized to nationalize silver. It is worth noting that the proposed silver bill does not bind the President to purchase silver. President Roosevelt also expressed his hope to submit a special message on war debts to Congress next week, but the President may not handle the war debt issue together with the silver issue. The debtor side declared that the proposed silver bill will stipulate that silver coins will be used as reserves to issue silver vouchers, with a ratio of US$1.29 per ounce. If the price per ounce is less than this amount, the difference will become the profit of the Treasury Department. It is estimated that 1,800,000,000 ounces of silver are needed to meet the 25% of total reserves. Well-informed sources claim that it is impossible to obtain such a huge amount. (National News Agency, 16th)

US Labor Unrest Expands: 7,000 Sailors Join Strike; 37 Merchant Ships Cease Operation 63

San Francisco. Approximately 7,000 merchant sailors have joined the dockworkers' strike, with 37 ships in the port of Seattle unable to depart because they have not unloaded their cargo. (Havas News Agency, 16th)

San Francisco. The Pacific Coast Seamen's Union decided today to express sympathy for the dockworkers' strike, which will completely paralyze Pacific shipping. Thousands of sailors and seamen in San Francisco and three thousand in other cities will join the strike. Other labor groups related to the shipping industry are also preparing to participate in the strike movement and have refused to handle ship cargo. Dockworkers have also expressed the same sentiment, and the situation is extremely concerning. Since the strike began a week ago, three people have died and nearly a hundred have been injured. Striking workers have repeatedly clashed with police. Dockworkers in ports in Baja California and workers along the Atlantic coast have also gone on strike, and it is feared that this unrest will soon expand to American ships overseas, although this is prohibited by law. Mail shipping companies are suffering losses of thousands of dollars every day, as many ships are stuck in port and cannot depart. Although mail shipping companies have offered high wages to workers and provided protection, the effect has been minimal. Fifty-two shipping companies in Portland and other places have temporarily suspended operations, and ships are congested in the port waiting to be unloaded. In San Francisco alone, thirty cargo ships are fully loaded but immobile. (National News Agency, 16th)

The auto industry was pleased to hear this, as the Fisher plant strike had been going on for a long time. Roosevelt Declares Management of Securities Transactions 65

(Washington) President Roosevelt today clearly stated his support for the management of securities exchanges by the Federal Trade Commission, as stipulated in the Securities Exchange Management Act passed by the House of Representatives, and does not support the establishment of another management committee, as proposed by the Senate. President Roosevelt also stated to members of both houses during the meeting that he wants the strict provisions of 45% margin in the bill passed by the House. The key points of this bill are: (1) all securities exchanges must register with the Federal Trade Commission; (2) the Federal Reserve Board is authorized to stipulate the minimum margin, with the margin being 45% in normal times; (3) any manipulation that can create artificial prices is prohibited. The House Agriculture Committee recently voted to apply this plan to cotton and grain transactions. (Reuters, 16th)

Russian Medical Scientist Discovers New Abdominal Surgery 69

(Moscow) Professor Gu Kovsky, a Soviet Russian surgeon, recently discovered a new abdominal dissection surgery, which he believes can save many lives. Mr. Gu Kovsky has been researching for many years and feels that most patients die because they cannot eat after abdominal dissection. Therefore, when Professor Gu first experimented, he planned to remedy this method. Before the dissection, he infused food into the intestines. This food is a nutritious "breakfast" such as butter, eggs, and milk. This nutritious food is sufficient to increase the patient's resistance, and can reduce the patient's mortality rate from 16% to 4.1% on average. Afterwards, light and soft nutritious foods are supplied to the patient before surgery, and then the patient can undergo local surgery. (National News Agency, 17th)

Zhao Zhiyou Discusses Waterway Management 72

(Nanjing) Zhao Zhiyou, Chairman of the Yangtze River Regulation Committee, departed from Wusongkou on the Lijiang ship to inspect the lower reaches of the Yangtze River and arrived in Nanjing. According to reports, the purpose of this inspection was to survey from Wusong, Chongming, Nantong, Jiangyin, Zhenjiang, to Nanjing. The collapse in the Langshan area is very dangerous, so personnel were sent to the area to conduct surveys and plan for proposed repairs. The collapse in this section is not extremely dangerous, and although repairs are necessary, no accidents should occur even if they are not carried out temporarily. However, the changes in the waterway from Langshan to Wusong are a serious problem. The section is fifty miles long, but the waterway has not changed. When Yangtze River merchant ships travel to this area, they dare not sail at night because the turning points of the changes are short and folded. Even a moment of carelessness can lead to grounding. This section of the waterway is constantly monitored by ships sent by the competent authorities, such as the Customs and Hydrographic Survey Bureau, to explore the waterway, so no dangers have been reported. Currently, when ships reach Langshan, they are afraid to sail and wait until dawn before raising anchor. The losses of this kind of company and passengers are considerable. Therefore, this regulation work is extremely important. 1. Starting from the upstream is the fundamental solution. 2. Further regulate the collapse on both banks of the downstream and build water barriers. After these two things are done, the water coming from the upstream can flow straight out, and the waterway will not change at any time. The council is currently organizing a downstream river management committee. After it is established and starts working, the waterway can gradually be stabilized. The siltation on the Zhenjiang riverbank is very serious, and the Jianglun ships cannot approach the pier. The council has also formulated a plan and requested the Jiangsu Provincial Government to regulate it within the possible scope. (Special Dispatch, 17th)

International Commercial Telegraph

Reuters Special Business Report for May 17th 101

Gold and Silver: London Gold Price: Today (May 17th), the London gold price was quoted at 136 shillings and 10 pence, up by a penny from yesterday.

London Silver Bar: Today (May 17th), the London silver market experienced widespread buying, with selling only from continental Europe. The quoted prices for both spot and futures were 19 pence and 6875, up by 5625 from yesterday.

New York Silver Bar: Today (May 17th), the silver market opened strongly but trading was flat. Sentiment was generally bullish due to developments in Washington and news from London that the United States was buying. Prices later eased due to profit-taking. There was neither exciting activity nor much speculative interest. Merchants are now waiting for President Roosevelt's announcement. Market prices are about 20 to 30 pounds lower than London. Distant futures opened at prices ranging from 71 to 95 pounds higher than yesterday's closing price.

Bombay Silver Bar: Today (May 17th), the Bombay silver market closed steadily. Spot prices rose by 11 annas to 53 rupees and 10 annas. Futures both rose by 10 annas.

Exchange Rates 102

British-American: Today (May 17th), the London foreign exchange market was uneventful. The British-American exchange rate opened at $5.11, up 125 from yesterday's US-British exchange rate closing price. It fluctuated erratically before settling at $5.11, the same as the opening price. One US dollar is equivalent to 3 shillings, 10 pence, and 972 British pounds.

British-French: Today (May 17th), the opening price was 77.34 francs, down 3 pounds from yesterday. It fell further to 77.28 francs in the afternoon and remained unchanged thereafter.

American-British: Today (May 17th), the New York exchange rate for British pounds opened at $5.10875, the same as yesterday's closing price. There were slight fluctuations in the morning, and then it was $5.11.

American-French: Today (May 17th), the New York exchange rate for French francs opened at 6.61, the same as yesterday's closing price.

Cotton and Wheat 103

American Cotton: Today (May 17th), the cotton market price rose sharply due to purchases by fellow bankers and foreigners, and speculators also bought in response to the news of the silver agreement. After the price increase, trading was thin, but the market was quite stable.

Indian Cotton: Today (May 17th), in the Bombay cotton market, Japanese and European exporters sold new white Luoqu cotton. Speculators purchased large quantities of July-August contracts. At closing, the July-August contract for white Luoqu cotton was priced at 197 rupees and 25, up 3 rupees.

British Cotton: Today (May 17th), in the Liverpool cotton market, the July contract was priced at 5.95 at 1:00 pm, up 6 pounds.

British Wheat: Today (May 17th), in the Liverpool wheat market, the July contract rose 75 to 4 shillings and 6 pence.

Rubber 104

London: Today (May 17th), the London rubber market was slightly weaker. At noon, the transaction price for July-September contracts was 6 pence and 125, down 125 from yesterday.

New York: Today (May 17th), the rubber market was stable. All sales were absorbed. Traders were greatly influenced by the silver news. Sentiment was good at the opening, but later became apprehensive.

Securities 105

New York: Today (May 17th), securities were firm, but trading was thin. After news of the silver legislation was approved, several mining stocks, led by American Smelting and Refining Company stock, rose by 25. Other securities also rose, but only slightly. With strict stock exchange regulations about to be implemented, the securities market may not have a lasting rebound. It is generally expected that trading will decline soon. A Painful Plea to the Motherland from Compatriots of the Northeast, Written in Blood and Tears 107

A Profound Lament on National Subjugation

Each Word a Tear, Worthy of Lament and Praise

Recently, a person from the Northeast secretly carried a letter to the fathers and elders of the nation from suffering compatriots in the Northeast. It recounts the pain of suffering national subjugation, earnestly hopes that the motherland will strive for strength, work together harmoniously to avoid the Northeast's fate, and even take further steps to recover lost territory. The letter is earnest, each word a tear, truly unbearable to finish reading. How should we, the people of the nation, strive to save the country, so as not to fail the earnest hopes of the suffering compatriots in the Northeast? The document is recorded below:

Alas, fathers and elders of the nation! Since our four provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe have been successively seized by the Japanese invaders, we feel like rabbits mourning the death of foxes, or things mourning the loss of their kind. Moreover, the bloodshed in Shanghai and the exposure of bones at the Great Wall, and the repeated harassment of Peiping and Tientsin, have caused our fathers and elders in the past two years to experience anxieties in their food, clothing, shelter, daily life, and mental state that cannot be described in words. So, why are we telling you this? Moreover, enduring humiliation to live under the trampling iron heel of Japan, unable to rise up, how can we have the face to look up to the fathers and elders of the country, raise our heads, and voice our opinions? However, the blind do not forget sight, and the lame do not forget walking. Being blind and lame is not what we wanted. Only because we are already blind and lame do we not want others to become blind and lame again. This is why we do not consider ourselves unsightly and tearfully offer sincere words to the fathers and elders of the nation. If we can continue with this great and thorough awakening, pool our wisdom and efforts, prepare in advance, and unite to resist foreign aggression, we can not only save ourselves from the disaster of being blinded and having our feet cut off, but also hope to rescue these blind and lame compatriots who have not forgotten sight and walking, and die returning to our ancestors. As the saying goes, "Learn from past mistakes to avoid future ones."

Speaking of our four provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe, in terms of territory, they are several times larger than the entire country of Japan. Counting the number of invaders who seized our Northeast, it was initially no more than ten thousand, while the population of our four northeastern provinces is as high as thirty-six million. Among them, the so-called formal army is no less than three hundred thousand strong. No matter how bad or insufficient our weapons and ammunition may be, if we had the heart and preparation to resist foreign aggression on normal days, then when the incident occurred, not to mention the formal army, even our thirty million people would have made it impossible for the Japanese invaders to use their strong armor and sharp weapons. As for the Battle of Rehe, if our troops had planned to throw their weapons on the main roads into Rehe to create obstacles, it would have taken the Japanese invaders several days to transport them away before they could occupy Chengde. There is absolutely no way it could have fallen as easily and quickly as it did. Therefore, Japan's current occupation of our Northeast is absolutely not due to the strength of its soldiers and the precision of its weapons. It is really because we had no heart or preparation to resist foreign aggression beforehand. This was an unexpected gain for Japan, which it initially did not expect. Now that it has obtained it, it will definitely do its best to manage it as its vast resource. However, giving an inch, they will take a mile. This is not related to personnel, but is the norm of the situation. Moreover, it was obtained easily and without any cost. Furthermore, international competition is becoming increasingly tense, and the environment forces them not to restrict themselves. This is why the Japanese invaders will take more planned steps to seize our North China. According to what we have heard and know, in the past two years, they have only used means of instigation, disturbance, making a big deal out of a small issue, and intimidation towards North China. Their main purpose is to use various forms of coercion to make our China first recognize the puppet state of Manchukuo. If the Manchukuo state they created cannot be recognized internationally, their management will be rootless, and at the very least, it will be resented by various countries. Therefore, for the past two years, they have spared no expense on publicity, liaison, and other expenses in Europe and the United States to seek recognition, but so far, there have been no tangible results. As a result, they have changed their strategy and decided to start with our China, because Chinese traitors can be lured with benefits, and the authorities can be threatened. They also know that our China cannot openly recognize it. Therefore, they raise negotiations on minor matters such as the exchange of trains and mail. If we refuse to accept them, they will accuse us of lacking sincerity and violating the spirit of the Tanggu Truce. If we accept these negotiations and establish some kind of agreement, they will recognize that our China has de facto recognition of Manchukuo, and will use this to further promote their cause and liaise with various countries, so that various countries have no excuse to refuse and there is no need to insist on the resolution of not recognizing Manchukuo. This is why they are so preoccupied with the issue of train and mail services and will not stop until they achieve it. Otherwise, since the September 18th Incident until today, the traffic inside and outside the customs has not stopped, especially for Japan, there is absolutely no obstacle. Why do they have to make such a resolute demand to us? We in the Northeast live in prison every day, like prisoners. This is not like the Japanese propaganda, the so-called paradise. Usually, we are always uneasy, not knowing when we will be framed by villains and suddenly thrown into prison. Even if we are released, our frightened souls are still uneasy. Therefore, although our bodies are under the violent trampling of the Japanese invaders every day, our hearts are always thinking of our entire country and the spirits of our Yellow Emperor ancestors in heaven. Therefore, regarding Japan's conspiracy, if we know anything, we must secretly report it. If we see anything, we must report it based on what we see. In our humble opinion, the issue of train and mail services is a small matter, but its impact is very large. Do not be lured or threatened by them and give them recognition or some kind of disguised agreement. No matter what form, once an agreement is established, not only will it not prevent the fall of North China, but it will also lead to the disaster of partitioning. At that time, various countries will believe that what Japan is publicizing is true. Regarding China, even if they do not want to believe that it does not have the qualifications to establish a country, they cannot. Since it is not enough to support and promote it, they can only adopt the principle of equal distribution of benefits. Indeed, when weighing two benefits, take the greater; when weighing two harms, take the lesser. They will partition China with Japan without the cost of losing arrows or broken arrows. If they restrict Japan for China, there is a risk of corpses and bloodshed. Regarding the advantages and disadvantages of this, people in Europe and the United States should not have any doubts. This is why we dare to assert that it will definitely lead to the disaster of partitioning. At that time, it is not known which country our fathers and elders will belong to, and the people of our four northeastern provinces will forever be slaves of Japanese slaves. Alas, how miserable!

Assuming that we firmly do not recognize the train and mail services, will North China not be in danger? Saying yes and no, it is inevitable that Japan will cause disturbances in North China. However, according to its plan and certain steps, and the strategies adopted for various countries, there will definitely be no immediate deployment of large armies to occupy North China. If Japan believes that occupying North China now is beneficial, then there would be no Tanggu Truce at all. The Tanggu Truce was not Japan being in a passive position or the success of our diplomatic negotiations, but Japan's policy of weighing the pros and cons and slightly slowing down its offensive against China. How can our diplomacy of seeking peace, begging for mercy, and holding our breath to listen to orders turn its fierce edge? Those who take the Tanggu Truce as a symbol of turning the crisis in North China into safety are shameless, and our life of stealing life and living in the Northeast is truly comparable to Lu and Wei. Furthermore, if we do not promise their train and mail services, they will occupy North China, and we will only have to do our best to resist. If we cannot resist, it is better to have it forcibly occupied like our Northeast than to recognize it and lose our diplomatic position, cut off the chance of recovery, and give various countries an excuse to partition it. Moreover, judging from their China policy, they do not have the determination to actively occupy North China at this time. Our fathers and elders should take this opportunity to prepare for resistance. Do not be afraid because it is coming and sit and wait for death. Do not be negligent because it has not yet arrived and do not prepare at all. During the September 18th Incident, the soldiers and civilians of our four northeastern provinces, both above and below, were suffering from this disease. This is why we today endure humiliation and do not avoid danger to enter the customs and present our foolishness to the fathers and elders of the nation.

If our fathers and elders do not discard words because of the person, and even more pity their urgency to prepare, silently organize, and mend the fold after the sheep is lost, it is not too late. Ten years ago, the environment of Italy, the Soviet Union, Germany, and other countries was several times worse than our country today. Only because they were able to unite and fight, they not only got out of trouble but also jumped up and became respected by the world. If our fathers and elders can abandon the prejudices of individualism and temporarily adopt a consistent attitude towards foreign countries, Heaven helps those who help themselves, and victory will surely be achieved. We are not just hoping for the fathers and elders and resigning ourselves to slavery. If this were the case, we would not have said these painful words to the fathers and elders. If we are asked why we do not rise up and fight immediately or all enter the customs to show our resistance, then it is a harsh demand. We are ashamed that before the September 18th Incident, we failed to prepare in advance and organize. When the disaster occurred, we responded in a hurry and were unable to accomplish anything. However, the spirit of unyielding has already been clearly demonstrated to the world by the three words "Volunteer Army." Now, if we want to solve the Northeast problem, it is not something that we can do alone. We must all have the determination to implement complete unity, act in unison, and wait for a suitable opportunity, so that we can recover it in one fell swoop. As for why we cannot all enter the customs, it is a matter of fact that is not allowed, not that we do not want to.

For the few Northeast intellectuals or those with considerable status who enter the customs, the country has no way to arrange for them, resulting in some being forced by life to go back and be heavily insulted by the Japanese. This is what we in the Northeast are most saddened and disappointed about. Not to mention that we are attached to our homeland and difficult for the old and weak to support, making it difficult to implement a scorched-earth policy. Even if it were implemented, does the country have a way to arrange for the thirty-six million people? If so, letting the land be inhabited by Japanese and Korean farmers is what Japan desires most. Therefore, we are forced by life to stay in the Northeast, or some may serve in the so-called Manchukuo, but they should not all be regarded as traitors and collaborators. Most of them hope to find an opportunity to repay China. This must be examined carefully. And at the very least, the country should not drive away the sparrows in droves. Therefore, for all the Northeast people who are now living in the customs, some are our fathers and brothers, and some are our sons and brothers, wandering like homeless dogs. Our country and the fathers and elders of North China should have pity and comfort them. Do not despise or exclude them because they have lost their provinces and homes, making them feel attacked from both inside and outside. This is what we especially entrust to the fathers and elders of the nation. Alas, fathers and elders, separated by a customs, we are close yet far apart. Raising our heads in the Central Plains, we have no tears to wipe away. One day, when you see fighters holding the flag of the Blue Sky, White Sun, and a Whole Earth, coming to shake our hands, you should know that our fathers and elders have worked hard and succeeded.

Japan's Policy of Immigrating to the Northeast 108

Immigrate Three Million People in Twenty Years

Organize a Joint Japanese-Puppet Immigration Company

Changchun Correspondence: The first step of Japan's plan to invade and occupy our Northeast has already achieved its goal. The second step of the plan is immigration, planning to immigrate three million people to the Northeast in twenty years. At present, it is proceeding steadily and without any relaxation. The Japanese Kwantung Army's Special Service Department has also ordered the puppet government to cooperate, ostensibly with both sides jointly establishing an immigration company. This plan was taken to Tokyo by Umetani, the immigration minister of the Japanese Kwantung Army's Special Service Department, for consultation with the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, the Ministry of Finance, and other relevant parties. It has been approved and encouraged by the Japanese government. The main points of the plan are: (1) The Manchuria Immigration Company will be jointly operated by Japan and the puppet government. (2) The capital is 20 million yuan, with the puppet country contributing 10 million yuan and Japan contributing 10 million yuan. (3) One million families will be moved within twenty years. The resettlement locations are mainly centered on the Hu-Hai and Zhai-Ke railways, relocating to the northeastern part of the puppet country. (4) Each family will have three members as a unit. (5) Each Japanese family relocating to puppet Manchuria will receive a government subsidy of 4,000 yuan in immigration fees.

Zhu and Zhang Arrive in Jiangxi to Meet Chiang: Zhu Jiahua Reports on Central Government Affairs on Behalf of Wang; Zhang Dingfan Discusses Post-Suppression and Rehabilitation in Jiangxi 109

Nanchang Correspondence: Minister of Transportation Zhu Jiahua arrived in Jiangxi on the morning of the 15th on the Yichang seaplane to meet Chiang and present important matters. The plane landed in the De Wai River around 1:00 PM. The head of the provincial postal bureau, the chief of the general affairs department of the general headquarters, and important figures from all walks of life welcomed him at the riverbank. After landing, Zhu went to Chiang's residence in De Wai to meet Chiang, reporting on the central government affairs on behalf of President Wang and asking for instructions on all matters related to the Ministry of Communications. It is said that Zhu will return to Nanjing to report after a short delay.

Central Committee member Zhang Dingfan, originally from Nanchang, Jiangxi, has not returned to his hometown since leaving Jiangxi in 1927. Now, due to important official matters, he met with Chairman Chiang on the 15th and took the early train from Xun to the province on the Nanxun Railway. The train arrived at Niuhang Station around 2:00 PM. Director Cai and Section Chief Wang of the General Headquarters welcomed and took care of him at the station. Zhang then crossed the river into the city with those who welcomed him and met with Chairman Xiong at the provincial government. After a brief chat, he stayed at Xiong's residence on Huanhu Road. Later, he visited Chiang to discuss everything. It is said that matters such as post-suppression and rehabilitation in Jiangxi and uniting the Southwest were discussed.

According to political sources, Minister of the Interior Huang Shaoxiong, Chairman of Shandong Province Han Fuqu, and the Panchen Lama will all come to Jiangxi to meet Chiang and report on various tasks (15th).

Guangdong Province Maintains the Salt Industry: New Organization Takes Over Salt Sales in Hunan; Merchants Allowed to Impose Additional Taxes to Repay Debts 110

Guangzhou Correspondence: After the collapse of Tailihe Company, which sold Guangdong salt in Hunan, after the absconding of responsible persons Zhao Jingshan and Wang Shaomu, the entire province's salt industry was affected. At the same time, government tax revenue was also significantly impacted. Because salt tax is a major source of national tax revenue, the company's collapse notwithstanding, future salt operations and tax payments must be actively maintained. Therefore, the salt industry and the Salt Transport Envoy's Office held repeated meetings to discuss methods to maintain the salt business. After official and commercial parties decided, starting from the 10th of this month, it was announced that the Tailihe Company would be abolished and replaced by the Joint Office Committee for the Transport and Sale of Salt in Southern Hunan, organized by the Guangzhou City Xiahe Salt Industry Association, the Tailihe Company Creditors' Group, and Tailihe Company shareholders. Each party will send five representatives, totaling fifteen members as the committee. All Guangdong salt transported to Hunan and the payment of unified taxes will be handled by this new organization. A Tailihe Company Account Clearing Committee will also be formed. The debts owed by Tailihe to outsiders and the accounts owed to them will be verified, recovered, and repaid by the Clearing Committee. The new merchants' salt tax amount will still be the previous 85,000 yuan per month (the original unified tax was 100,000 yuan, but due to sluggish salt sales in southern Hunan, it was approved to reduce it by 15,000 yuan per month). However, now it is the off-season, and from April to July, only 60,000 yuan can be sold each month. August is the peak season, at which time it can be made up for. New merchants will resume business and allocation from the 10th. In the future, taxes will be paid monthly without delay. The former company owed more than 300,000 yuan in taxes for April, and 1 million yuan in promissory notes borrowed before the year, including principal and interest. New merchants will be allowed to impose an additional five jiao per bag of salt, which will be repaid by the Clearing Committee in installments until it is paid off. It is estimated that it can be repaid in one year or a year and a half. After the new merchants take over, Tailihe Company has also been closed. All previous expenses have been greatly reduced. The former three detachments of salt police on the North River have now been reduced to one detachment. Offices in various places have also reduced office expenses. The transportation routes still enter southern Hunan in two ways: one through the North River and one through the West River, passing through Guangxi. Currently, there are 32 counties in the area selling Guangdong salt in southern Hunan, but the sales market is weaker than before. The current market price of salt is about five to six yuan per bag (12th).

Songjiang: Provincial Order to Organize Car Roads 111

Since the opening of the Shanghai-Hangzhou National Highway to traffic, there has been a constant flow of vehicles in and out. Trees are planted on both sides of the road to embellish the scenery. The seawalls in Caoging, Zhaolin, and Jinshanwei in this county are the necessary places for the National Highway to pass. The Provincial Department of Construction specially notified the county government that the Beijing-Hangzhou, Shanghai-Jurong, Shanghai-Hangzhou, and Suzhou-Jiaxing four roads will hold the Southeast Touring Exhibition in June. At that time, Chairman Chiang will personally participate. The Shanghai-Hangzhou National Highway is also within the ring line. For the section of the National Highway passing through the county, if the branches of the trees planted on both sides are withered, they should be pruned immediately. If there are any missing trees, they should be quickly replanted to enhance the view. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Jin instructed patrol officer Li Yihua to be responsible for handling it and to submit a report.

Haimen: Two Wanted Bandits Arrested in Shanghai 112

The two wanted bandits of this county, Lu Maoping and Wang Jinyue, colluded in July last year to confiscate two rifles from the Yong'an Bridge Security Team of the Fourth District and robbed the house of Fan Chongwen in the same district, killing Fan Chongwen, his wife, and Fan Chengqing. The county government has been strictly searching for them without success. A few days ago, the two criminals Lu and Wang were arrested by the Shanghai-Songhu Garrison Headquarters in Shanghai for endangering the Republic of China. After interrogation by the headquarters, it was deemed necessary to summon the family members of the victim Fan Chongwen. Yesterday, they specially checked and sent summons and sent a letter to the county government of this county, ordering the police to summon Fan Huangshi, Fan Chenglong, and Fan Qizhen to the headquarters for questioning in order to handle the case according to law.

Kunshan: Lujia Port to Build a Large Factory 113

Recently, Mr. Huang Hongjun, the general manager of the Shanghai China Underwear Company, purchased 400 mu of land along the Wusong River in Lujia Port Town, the Autonomous Experiment Zone of this county, and prepared to raise 3 million yuan to build a large factory such as a fine yarn dyeing factory to resist the dumping of foreign goods. It is now learned that the district chief of the district, Zhu Wenyuan, and local gentry and landlords are making every effort to mediate, and all negotiations have been completed. Yesterday (the 14th), Mr. Huang came to Lu and paid the land price at the district office and signed the contract. Construction will begin after the tombs are cleaned.

Wuxi: The Reaction to the Prohibition of Rented Factories 114

In recent years, the rural economy has gone bankrupt, resulting in sluggishness in all industries, and the failure of silk factories is especially unbearable. Since the beginning of spring, only a dozen or so factories have started up, but silk sales are sluggish, making it difficult to maintain them. With a shortage of capital, silk factories have had the phenomenon of owing wages. The county government of this county has specially stipulated provisional measures for prohibiting rented silk factories, in order to prevent speculative silk factories. After being approved by the provincial government for implementation, it is now found that among the factories that have started operation in this county, except for Huaxin, Jinji, Yongtai, Longchang, Yongsheng, Yongji, Ganshen, and Gantai, which have built their own factory buildings and installed silk reeling machines, the remaining Dechang, Yuji, Dacheng, Qingfengsheng, Qingyu, Xinyi, and Hefeng are all rented. It is inevitable that they will be stretched thin with this method. Yesterday, they gathered to discuss countermeasures and decided to first send a letter to the Silk Factory Association, forwarding it to the county government, requesting them to consider the difficulties of the merchants renting factories and to withdraw the order, and to postpone the provisional measures for prohibiting rented silk factories. Once business turns around and the economy is slightly better, they will follow the measures to maintain the livelihood of tens of thousands of workers.

Changshu: Fushan Pond Project Completed and Dam Opened 115

The Fushan Pond of this county was previously difficult for boats to pass through due to the accumulation of tidal mud. The dredging association allocated funds for dredging, which started on the first day of last month. Later, the person in charge was changed, and the weather was not sunny, so it was extended to the middle of this month and had not been completed. However, recently, it is the peak season of the Fushan yellow croaker market, and those who rely on the passage of ships through the Fushan Pond are very eager, and the farmland along the pond also needs irrigation. Therefore, they requested the authorities to speed up the completion of the project. The Provincial Department of Construction specially sent technician Gao Zhongyuan to Changshu to inspect and accept the project. He went to inspect on the 14th and believed that the bottom of the river and the surface of the river did not meet the original plan and would not be accepted. Later, the authorities increased wages and ordered to rush the excavation. The project was completed at noon on the 17th, and it was decided to break the dam at 5:00 PM that afternoon when the tide rises, so that ships can pass through.

Aftermath of the Fire at Canghai Temple

The Canghai Temple, one of the four major monasteries on the top of Yushan Mountain in this county, was destroyed by fire after the Shangyi incense offering. All the essence of the temple was lost, and the loss was not small. It is not easy to repair the temple now. Monk Zhiguang intends to raise funds for reconstruction in order to protect the ancient temple of Yushan. It is now learned that there are more than 400 incense societies in the temple. Zhiguang plans to summon the heads of the societies to gather on the mountain to discuss aftermath measures.

Changzhou: Two Sailing Ships Robbed by Bandits 116

Two sailing ships from Yixing Heqiao and Qitingqiao to Changzhou set sail one after another in the town on the 15th and anchored overnight at Wantazhen in Changjing. At dawn on the 16th, the two ships continued to sail at the same time. Unexpectedly, when passing through the Shiwudong Bridge area about three miles from the town, a small boat suddenly sailed towards them and ordered them to dock. The boat crew docked in the river, and then more than a dozen bandits jumped onto the ship and searched wantonly in the two ships. None of the passengers on the ship were spared. At that time, two passengers resisted and were shot and injured. All the goods in the ship were robbed. Afterwards, the ship still sailed to Changzhou. The shipping association reported to the county government to arrest the bandits.

Zhenjiang: Investigation and Prohibition of Scientific Spiritual Divination Charts 117

The Jiangsu Provincial Party Department found that the scientific spiritual divination charts that have been popular in the city recently have a wide sales volume. After investigating its content, it is actually promoting spiritual divination and superstition in the name of science. It is already similar to what wizards and alchemists do, and its instructions are even more absurd and unbelievable. Regardless of the fact that today's natural sciences such as psychology, physiology, and anatomy are flourishing and progressing, the consciousness and spiritual phenomena of human beings can be explained by natural sciences, and the theory of the so-called soul is fundamentally untenable. Moreover, at a time when we are advocating the popularization of scientific knowledge among the people and the New Life Movement, it is not appropriate to let it spread widely. It is reported that in addition to the provincial government ordering bookstores to be prohibited from selling the charts, the provincial party department has also ordered the county party departments to cooperate with the local government to strictly ban them in order to prevent the spread of superstition.

Pinghu: A Trafficked Girl Intercepted at the Railway Station 118

The customs of Pinghu are extremely simple and honest, but recently young people have become accustomed to vanity, and the ethos has changed drastically. There are not a few rural girls who are trafficked abroad and forced into prostitution in Shanghai. Yesterday afternoon, when the train from Pinghu to Shanghai was about to depart, there was a girl in front of the railway station who looked flustered and as if she was waiting for someone. It happened to be seen by the police officer on duty there, who stepped forward to question her. She claimed to be surnamed Chen, living in Ximen in the city, and was about to go to Zha with her brother for sightseeing. When asked where her brother was, she said he was sipping tea in a nearby teahouse. The police officer ordered her to prove it. The girl pointed to a pockmarked man and said it was him. The police officer questioned him about his surname. He claimed to be named Zhou Mingxiang and said that the girl was a neighbor, and they were going to Shanghai together. The police officer suspected that there was a case of abduction because the words of both parties did not match. They were detained at the Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Funing: Private Tutor Assassinated 119

In the Sifanggang area of the Sixth District of this county, Jiang Weifu, the son of Jiang Yushu, was teaching at the house of Liu Gukun in the Liu family compound. On the night of April 26, Weifu suddenly disappeared. Yesterday, his father hired a boat to Funing to look for him. When passing through the Xiaoyaowan area, he saw a section of a corpse on the Chai beach next to a broken tomb, as well as two human legs and one human arm. He went to the corpse to identify it carefully and confirmed that it was the body of his son. The remaining head and arm have not yet been found. The cause of death is rumored to be due to adultery. He has already reported the case to the county government yesterday. The county government has now sent personnel to the site to investigate along with a scribe.

Hangzhou: A Major Fire Late at Night in Baoji Guan Lane 120

The material warehouse in the gatehouse at No. 32 and No. 34, Xiaojingtou, Baoji Guan Lane, Hangzhou City, was opened by resident Tong Huixing, and the business was quite good. At 1:40 AM on the 16th, a sudden fire broke out due to carelessness. Neighbors were awakened from their dreams and rushed to rescue. However, the fire was fierce. After the fire brigade and others tried their best to put out the fire, it was extinguished after burning for about two hours. It is estimated that two gatehouses and three flat halls were burned, with a loss of more than 4,000 yuan.

Provincial Government Awards Plaque to Li Fangxiao

Ding Qiuzhen, the leader of the Phoenix Mosque in Hangzhou City, submitted a request to the provincial government to award an honorary plaque to Li Fangxiao, a Henan native and leader residing in the temple, because he is well-versed in health preservation and is now 112 years old and still has light hands and feet, which can be called a human auspicious sign. The provincial government ordered the municipal government to verify that it was true. Yesterday, the province issued a plaque with the four characters "Luo Zhong Yuan Shuang" and ordered the municipal government to hand it over to the recipient.

Hefei: Six Bandits Executed by Firing Squad 121

The bandits who robbed the home of Gao Dongyai, a resident next to the Dongyue Temple in Dongmen, were arrested by the Second Battalion of the Third Regiment of the 193rd Brigade of the 65th Division of the garrison army. Liu Xuecheng, Zhou Shengsan, Wang Chunhai, Yang Sitao, Yang Xiaoqiang, and Yang Xiuqi, confessed to participating in the robbery and sharing the loot without denying it. They were sentenced to death. On the 11th, the six bandits were escorted back to Hefei, and on the 12th at noon, they were tied to the Shuiguan outside the Dongmen and executed by firing squad.

Local News

Shanghai-Yantai-Dagu Submarine Cable Contract Expires; Government to Take Over Management Starting Tomorrow; Ministry of Transportation Cables Telegraph Bureau to Take Charge; Great Northern and Great Eastern Cease Sending Domestic Telegrams on the Line 122

Our country's Shanghai-Yantai-Dagu submarine cable line was previously entrusted to the Great Northern and Great Eastern Telegraph Companies for management. Telegrams transmitted via this submarine cable could also be entrusted to the submarine cable telegraph offices for collection and delivery. From the 20th of this month, the Ministry of Transportation will take back the submarine cable for self-management. All telegrams between Shanghai and various places in North China, which are transmitted via the Shanghai-Yantai-Dagu submarine cable, will be received and delivered by the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau. A reporter from the Shen Shi News Agency specially investigated and reported the following yesterday:

Officially Taking Over Tomorrow Night 123

The Shanghai-Yantai-Dagu submarine cable line was installed by the Great Northern and Great Eastern Companies during the Boxer Rebellion in the Guangxu period of the Qing Dynasty without the consent of our government. The value is estimated to be several million yuan. After our discovery and negotiation, we offered to buy it back. Before the payment was cleared, the companies temporarily managed it. The payment was deducted from the cable fee payable to the Ministry of Transportation on time, with a contract period of 30 years. After one extension, it expired on May 20th of this year. All payments have been fully paid. The Ministry of Transportation specifically cabled the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau's submarine cable engineers to take charge and implement the recovery of management rights from the companies at 12:00 pm on the 19th. From 1:00 am on the 20th, all telegrams sent and received on the line will be fully negotiated and handled by the company.

Original Text of the Ministry of Transportation's Cable 124

The Ministry of Transportation, for the purpose of taking over the Shanghai-Yantai-Dagu submarine cable line, yesterday ordered the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau and the International Radio Station: "The Shanghai-Yantai-Dagu submarine cable line, managed by the Great Northern and Great Eastern Telegraph Companies, has been ordered by this Ministry to be taken back for self-management by submarine cable engineers Shen Fuhai, Lin Zhaoxiang, Wu Bonian, etc., on May 20th. From that day onwards, the International Bureau's Great Northern and Great Eastern internal cable telegrams should cease to send and receive domestic telegrams, except for those transmitted via the Shanghai-Hong Kong submarine cable. All domestic telegrams to and from North China originally transmitted via the Shanghai-Yantai-Dagu submarine cable line should be received and delivered by the bureau. You are required to comply immediately and, together with the International Bureau, publish advertisements in the Shanghai Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao, Dalu Bao, and Zi Lin Western Newspaper for three days before May 20th to inform the public." Minister of Transportation Zhu Jia驊.

Joint Notice from Two Bureaus 125

The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau of the Ministry of Transportation and the International Telecommunications Bureau, after receiving the order, jointly issued a notice yesterday: "Recently, we received an order from the Ministry of Transportation, which stated: 'The Shanghai-Yantai-Dagu submarine cable line, managed by the Great Northern and Great Eastern Telegraph Companies, is scheduled to be taken over on May 20th. From that day onwards, all domestic telegrams to and from the companies should cease to be sent and received, except for those transmitted via the Shanghai-Hong Kong submarine cable. They should all be received and transmitted by this bureau, etc.' Joint notice to inform the public. Hereafter, all merchants who specialize in sending telegrams to North China, if they have not yet deposited funds and opened accounts at the Shanghai Telegraph Bureau, are requested to come to the Telegraph Bureau from now on to pay the deposit and obtain a passbook as required." This announcement.

Kong Xiangxi Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday; Returns to Beijing Immediately to Attend the National Financial Conference 126

According to the Central News Agency, Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, after inspecting the financial situation in the provinces of Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan, left Beijing by night train for Shanghai on the night before last. He arrived at the Zhenru Station at 7:25 am yesterday and went directly to his private residence on West Yanan Road to rest. At noon, he went to the Central Bank to work. At 5:00 pm, he met with reporters from various newspapers at the Central Bank. Kong will return to Beijing within a few days to preside over the National Financial Conference. The following is a record of Kong's remarks:

Financial Situation in Four Provinces Has Improved 127

According to Kong, during his visit to the provinces of Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan, he inspected the financial situation in each province. When passing through Anhui, he injured his foot due to carelessness. After arriving in Jiangxi, he immediately met with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. He discussed in detail the matters concerning the suppression of bandits and the various issues of the National Economic Council. He also discussed inviting five experts from the Economic Council's Health and Highway departments to discuss the future work progress. After arriving in Wuhan, he met with Zhang Hanqing and inspected the financial revenue and expenditure situation in Hubei Province. He then accepted the invitation of Chairman He of Hunan Province and flew to Hunan to meet with him for a short stay before returning to Wuhan. He then took the Customs Maritime Star patrol ship and returned to Beijing with Rogers, an American silver expert. During the journey, he exchanged detailed opinions on silver with Rogers on the ship. Although the inspection trip only covered the four provinces of Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Hunan, he believes that the financial situation in these four provinces has greatly improved compared to the past. As for the current revenue and expenditure situation in the four provinces, Hubei and Hunan can balance their revenue and expenditure. Anhui Province feels a slight shortage due to the expenses of the security corps. Jiangxi is in a special environment, and of course, revenue cannot meet expenditure.

Rectification Measures Will Be Submitted to the Assembly 128

As for the rectification of the finances of various provinces, Kong believes that this issue is very broad and cannot be resolved in a few words. However, in a nutshell, to rectify the finances of various provinces, we must first understand the financial situation of each province. There is no denying that the finances of each province urgently need rectification. Even the central government's finances urgently need rectification. The rectification strategy should also be determined according to the environment of each province. For example, the collection of land tax in Hubei Province is not calculated by the acre, but by the amount of grain sown per field. And there is no reliable survey of the amount of grain sown. This situation must be reformed immediately. This issue will be discussed at the National Financial Conference, which will open on the 21st of this month. Kong himself has decided to go to Beijing to preside over the meeting before the conference. Financial authorities from various provinces and cities have flocked to Beijing to attend.

Suma Visits Kong, Does Not Discuss Foreign Debt 129

According to Kong, the Japanese Consul in Beijing, Suma, visited him in Beijing on the 16th as a routine courtesy visit. He inquired about his recent trip to various provinces and his health. The issue of foreign debt was never mentioned. The report that Suma's visit was to discuss the reorganization of foreign debt is not accurate. If the Japanese side wants to request the reorganization of foreign debt, there are responsible personnel to directly contact the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. There is no need for Suma to discuss with him. Moreover, there is a committee for reorganizing domestic and foreign debt. Therefore, the rumors are not true.

Construction Company is Entirely Chinese-Owned 130

Kong also said that the capital of the Construction Bank is entirely Chinese-owned. However, if a large amount of capital is needed in the future for investment, foreign capital can be absorbed under appropriate conditions. As for the rumor that the French person Monna has colluded with the Japanese to invest in the Construction Company, it is not accurate. Kong then answered reporters' questions, saying that the exact date of Lassiman's visit to China is still undecided. The rumor that Liu Zhi, chairman of the Henan Provincial Government, will be transferred to chairman of Hunan Province is even more unfounded.

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Sends Six Special Representatives Overseas Tomorrow Afternoon; Four Hai Class Ships Being Built in England; All Expected to Arrive in Shanghai This Year 132

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is using funds borrowed from the Sino-British Boxer Indemnity to build four new Hai Class ships in England. The company has appointed technicians and marine engineers to go to England for practical training, and they will set sail tomorrow afternoon. The details are as follows:

Two Shipyards Undertake Construction 133

Because all four new Hai Class ships must be completed this year, two ships are being built by Swan Hunnfer & Wigham Richardsou in London, England, and two ships are also being built by Barclay Curled & C in Glasgow, Scotland. Construction by two shipyards will be faster. It was initially heard that two ships would be completed first this year. Now, according to the telegram from the construction supervisor, the two shipyards are stepping up construction, and the four new ships are scheduled to be fully completed and arrive in Shanghai within the year.

All Arrive Within the Year 134

The Haiyuan and Haiheng ships will be completed simultaneously in mid-November of this year and sail to Shanghai. Therefore, ship owners Ma Jiajun and Teng Shibiao, who were appointed by the company, will go to England in August to escort the two new ships to Shanghai. The Haili and Haizhen ships will be completed a month later, so they can also arrive in Shanghai in late December. The crew and captains of these four new ships will be appointed after they arrive. The business section has decided to abolish the contract system and appoint a purser to report and reimburse expenses to the company.

Farewell Banquet the Night Before Last 135

Because the machinery and engines of the four new ships being built in England are all new models, the company first sent technician Huang Zonglun, chief engineer Zhang Guoquan, marine engineers Shi Ruichang and Li Changwen, and Zhou Yanjin and Wang Chengzhu, graduates of the marine engineering program at the Wusong Merchant Marine School. It is the first time that a Chinese shipping company has sent technical personnel to foreign shipyards to learn about marine engineering. Therefore, Liu Hongsheng, general manager of China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, hosted a banquet at his residence at 6:00 pm the day before yesterday to bid farewell to the six men. Zhao Yuntai and Zhou Houkun, heads of the shipbuilding department, were also invited to attend. During the banquet, they were encouraged to pay attention to the technology of the new machinery. Although the practical training time is not long, they will become the company's basic technical experts when they return to China with the ships in the future. Department heads Zhao and Zhou also made encouraging remarks.

Set Sail Tomorrow Afternoon 136

Huang Zonglun and the others have all completed their original duties (shipbuilding technician, director of the inland shipping factory) and handed them over to Mr. Zhang, who will act on their behalf. Zhang Guoquan has also relinquished his duties as chief engineer of the Jiahe ship. All procedures have been completed. The accounting department has also purchased British and French currency on their behalf. All procedures were completed yesterday. Ship tickets were purchased on the French postal ship Xidaosis No. 2, which is scheduled to board the ship at noon tomorrow and leave Shanghai at 2:00 pm in the afternoon. Huang and the others will take the designs and logos of the four new ships to England. The six men will first go to Marseille and then to London and Scotland. All relevant shipyards have been notified.

Sales of British and American Chinese Tea; British Merchants Willing to Promote Improved Black Tea; American Merchants Warns in Letter About Pingshui Green Tea 146

In recent years, the export of Chinese tea to foreign markets has been declining due to poor quality and the dumping of Indian and Ceylon tea. British and American countries have almost abandoned it. The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry, in view of this, is actively engaged in inspection and improvement, and cooperates with tea merchants in producing areas to organize cooperatives. Regarding the black tea from Ningzhou, Qimen, and other places, the foreign firm Jinlong Yangxing in Shanghai is very appreciative and is willing to send it to London for promotion. As for the Pingshui green tea in Zhejiang, a letter from New York states that the Pingshui tea is terrible and unacceptable to customers. If it is not actively improved, it will disappear. The details are as follows:

Page 10

Establishing Improvement Farms 147

The Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry believes that the quality of China's exported tea has been declining year by year, resulting in a continuous decline in export volume and sales price. If improvements are not made, there will be no foothold in international trade. Therefore, in addition to actively engaging in inspection work, it has recently paid special attention to improving the quality of tea in various regions. It has also cooperated with the Department of Construction of Anhui Province to operate Qimen Tea Improvement Farms and organized many production and sales cooperatives in order to reduce costs. In addition, it has jointly established a tea industry improvement farm in Ningzhou with the Central Agricultural Experiment Institute of the Ministry of Industry and the Hankou Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry. The newly produced black tea from the farm this year is of exceptionally high quality and can compete with Indian and Ceylon black tea. A Hankou foreign firm offered 120 yuan (the market price of ordinary Ningzhou black tea is only 60-70 yuan). If it can be gradually improved, tea merchants can obtain great benefits.

Willing to Promote 148

Jinlong Yangxing sent a letter to the bureau yesterday, expressing its willingness to send the black tea to London for promotion as advertising. The original letter stated: "To the Executive Director of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau, we are deeply grateful for the three types of Ningzhou black tea that you have jointly produced at the tea improvement farm. We congratulate you on producing such good tea. Do you have this tea available now? What is the quantity? We believe that our company can ship several boxes each of this imitation Ceylon black tea and the other two types to London and sell them at the tea public auction as advertising for Chinese tea. Our company is confident that the goods can be sold at a good price. This proves that if tea farmers in the interior can carefully produce tea, they can get high rewards."

Letter from New York 149

The United States has a very large demand for green tea. Pingshui tea from various counties in Shaoxing, Zhejiang, is a major commodity sold in the United States. However, in recent years, the products have become increasingly inferior, and exports have decreased. A certain company in New York sent a letter to the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau of the Ministry of Industry yesterday, stating: "Director, we are very grateful for your bureau's 1933 export statistics. This book is very helpful to this industry. After receiving this book, we also learned that your office has established a tea experiment farm. We wish your farm can produce excellent Chinese tea this season. Out of our love for your bureau, we would like to offer a humble opinion, which may be of help to the improvement of Chinese tea. The quantity of Chinese tea imported into the United States is still declining. Last year, the quality of Huzhou and Pingshui green tea was significantly worse than the previous year, which made our customers very unhappy. They told us that if the quality of Pingshui tea is still poor this year, they will not buy Pingshui tea and will only buy a small amount of Huzhou tea. The situation is serious, and we can only hope that your office can produce good tea for sale. We look forward to it very much."
