Lake Society Public Memorial Service: Lake Society members, fellow townsmen in Shanghai, small and medium-sized schools from Huzhou in Shanghai, and Jingxiong Girls' School decided to hold a public memorial service at the Chen Qimei Memorial Hall on Beijing Road at 9:00 AM today. The order of the public memorial service is as follows: (1) Opening of the meeting; (2) Playing music; (3) Singing the party song; (4) Paying the highest respect to the national flag and party flag and the portrait of the Premier; (5) The chairman respectfully reads the Premier's will; (6) Silent tribute; (7) Public memorial service: (A) Offering flowers; (B) Reading the memorial text; (C) Paying respects to the portrait of the late Chen Qimei; (D) Singing the mourning song; (8) Reporting on the deeds of the martyr; (9) Speech; (10) Playing music and closing the meeting. A hygiene lecture will also be held tonight.

City-Wide Security: The Songhu Garrison Headquarters, the Security Department, the Public Security Bureau, and other military and police agencies, considering today as a commemorative day, followed the security measures of May, ordering their subordinates to strengthen security to prevent unscrupulous elements from taking the opportunity to cause disturbances. The police authorities of the Public Concession and the French Concession also dispatched Chinese and Western detectives today to strengthen prevention to maintain public order.

Longhua District: Automatic Telephone Service to Be Activated Tomorrow; Rumors of Direct Connection Machines for Concession Telephones Are Untrue; The Pujiang River Submarine Cable Is Not Yet Repaired 151

The Longhua District automatic telephone conversion project of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications has been completed and will officially open for calls on the 19th. Details are as follows:

Project Completed, Trial Calls 152

The Telephone Bureau has seen a flourishing situation in the Longhua area and a daily increase in the number of telephone subscribers. The original common battery telephone exchange was also obsolete. Therefore, in March of this year, the Ministry of Communications purchased an automatic telephone exchange with 250 lines from the American Automatic Telephone Company. Since dismantling and installation, it was completed last week. The previous two days, Yu Bingjian, Chief Engineer of the Telephone Bureau, personally went there to conduct trial calls with the North and South cities, and the results were quite good. Today and tomorrow, trial calls will continue with the Shanghai West Zhenru Jiangwan Wusong areas. It is reported that this telephone exchange is sufficient for three years of need.

Calls on the 19th 153

All eighty-odd telephone sets have been converted last week. The old telephones that were removed will be used in the Minhang District in the future. The Telephone Bureau believes that automatic telephone exchanges and other equipment are more numerous than common battery equipment. The original building was difficult to manage. A new building was specially expanded on the left side of the original bureau to house the automatic telephone equipment and officially open the line at 11:00 PM on the 19th (Saturday). The first number was uniformly changed to "68," and the last three digits were also reorganized in the same way as other districts.

Submarine Cable Not Recovered 154

It has been rumored that the Telephone Bureau intends to switch to direct calls on the 19th for the convenience of city communications and telephones to the concessions, with a direct reporting machine and a counting machine monitoring platform. In the future, you can dial "0" and then dial the concession number to connect (because the original number was called out). However, the relevant parties absolutely denied this. As for the Pujiang submarine cable, after being repeatedly broken, the Telephone Bureau has not yet recovered it. At the same time, in order to repair it as soon as possible to facilitate telephone communication, it is specially supervising the workers to speed up repairs. If the weather is clear tomorrow, it can be repaired the day after tomorrow. Telephone communication between the concession and Pudong is still smooth, and only a major obstacle has occurred between the North and South cities and Pudong.

Tobacco Leaf Association Submits to the Taxation Department: Suggesting Improving Domestic Tobacco Leaves and Requesting Appropriation to Establish Curing Factories 155

Ding Zhenbo, standing committee member of the Shanghai Chinese Tobacco Leaf Trade Association, submitted a request to the Taxation Department yesterday, suggesting improving domestic tobacco leaves and requesting that a portion of the government's appropriation to the Tobacco Factory Association be allocated for the organization of curing factories. The original letter was obtained and recorded below. Presented as a proposal for organizing tobacco, requesting examination and approval. I, in private, have investigated that our country is vast and abundant, with rich agricultural products. The needs of the people are fully self-sufficient. Since the opening of the sea ban, foreign goods have been increasing daily, using sophisticated techniques and abundant capital for dumping. Looking back at the products of our country, they stick to the old ways and do not know how to improve, so that foreign goods sell well and domestic goods have almost no foothold. The annual outflow is increasing more and more, which makes me anxious and painful to speak of. I have investigated that the tobacco leaves produced in our country were initially used exclusively for tobacco pipe shops to make dry tobacco. Since the opening of the sea, the better ones have been packaged and sold abroad, such as to Egypt and Germany, and the second-best to Japan and the three northeastern provinces. Since the Republic of China, American tobacco seeds have been distributed in Fengyang County, Anhui Province. Although the tobacco color and texture are good, the smell is not as good as American products. Later, they were planted in prefectures and counties in Shandong Province, but the smell was also not as good as American tobacco. Finally, they were planted in Xiang County, Henan Province, and other places, and the color, texture, and taste were all qualified. Since the National Government established its capital in Nanjing and the Taxation Department was established, our country's tobacco leaves have been divided into two types: local tobacco and miscellaneous tobacco. The difference is that local tobacco is dried in the sun, and the smoke is baked using local methods. There are several reasons why local tobacco cannot be developed in recent years: (1) Local tobacco is divided into red tobacco and white tobacco. Red tobacco is from Guangfeng, Tongxiang, etc., and most of it is sold to Egypt, the Netherlands, and other countries. White tobacco is from Huanggang, Xinchang, Fengzhou, etc., and most of it is sold to Germany, the Netherlands, etc. The second-best is exclusively sold to various inland tobacco pipe shops for the manufacture of dry tobacco, such as Champion, Susong, etc., and sold to Japan, the three northeastern provinces, and various inland tobacco pipe shops. Now, because cigarette production is increasing year by year, local tobacco, because it is dried in the sun, does not have the right smell for cigarette raw materials, so sales are gradually declining. (2) Foreign countries are determined to exclude foreigners, and the import tax on local tobacco is gradually increasing, which has dealt a major blow to domestic tobacco leaves, so the quantity has been very small in recent years. (3) In the Northeast, the puppet Manchukuo is independent, and the import tariff has increased to twelve yuan and five jiao per picul. Moreover, Japan, Korea, and other places also have newly produced American tobacco leaves. Not only are they for their own use, but they are also allowed to supply the puppet Manchukuo, and Shanghai also imports and dumps them. The problem with our production method is that it is not as good as theirs. For example, if the cultivation is proper and scientific methods are used for baking, domestic tobacco leaves will of course not be comparable to them. If the country is to plan for the present, it should immediately catch up, improve domestic tobacco leaves, and start with American flue-cured tobacco. It is estimated that about 100,000 barrels of American tobacco are imported each year, each barrel weighing about 1,000 pounds, totaling 100 million pounds. The average price is about 5 jiao per pound, totaling more than 50 million yuan. Large factories in Britain, the United States, etc. directly purchase from the United States, which is not included in the count. Now, those who manufacture cigarettes use about 70% American tobacco, and only 30% of our country's flue-cured tobacco. There are several reasons why we cannot use more of our country's flue-cured tobacco: (1) For example, Henan flue-cured tobacco has the best quality and taste for cigarette raw materials, but the tobacco seeds have not been changed for many years, and no one guides the cultivation. Although agricultural products depend on the abundance or scarcity of the weather, it is also necessary to study and quickly improve them. (1) Baking is done using local methods, the heat cannot be consistent, and it often spoils quickly, and the color and aroma gradually disappear. Not only is it difficult to sell at a good price, but there is also no way to turn around in terms of finance. (3) The packaging by merchants is inconsistent from top to bottom. For example, tobacco factories need first-class, but there are still second-class mixed in, deceiving themselves and others. This is the main reason for the failure of the old Chinese business. Now, at a time when businesses from various countries are competing, it is difficult to rectify without unity, and rectification cannot be effective without the cooperation of the government and the people. Flue-cured tobacco, after organization and improvement, its future development is of course promising. For example, if cigarette companies use more flue-cured tobacco, our country's outflow can be reduced by tens of millions of yuan. Not only will the rural economy rely on turning around, but government tax revenue can also be increased a lot. The national treasury and people's livelihood will benefit from both. Therefore, improvement and organization are urgent tasks at present. The proposed methods are listed in several points below: (1) Distributing seeds: First, purchase American tobacco seeds and distribute them to farmers so that production can be abundant. (2) Establishing curing factories: This is the fundamental foundation for flue-cured tobacco and taxation. All flue-cured tobacco must be baked nearby to prevent spoilage over time. Tobacco that has been baked can be stored for as long as six years, and the color and aroma can be preserved. Henan flue-cured tobacco, if baked with machines, is no less than imported American tobacco. (3) The organization of curing factories, or officials and merchants each recognize their two official shares, and the annual interest and surplus profits obtained are used for cultivating and guiding farmers and raising seeds, so that the fundamental of flue-cured tobacco is permanently guaranteed. Merchant shares, in addition to extracting a certain amount for public accumulation, are distributed according to shares. (4) The capital of the curing factory must not be used for flue-cured tobacco transactions, so as to avoid cutting off flue-cured tobacco sales. As for the packaging layer, the curing factory should select impartially to avoid the disadvantages of inconsistent tops and bottoms of each package. The grades are selected separately by the vendors, so that all manufacturers and purchasers have standards to follow. (5) If the curing factory is established, the tax revenue can be collected without any leaks, and the tobacco industry can also compete with foreign goods. (6) The construction cost of the curing factory is about 300,000 yuan. The business regulations and construction plan will be presented in detail later. It was previously heard that the Ministry of Finance allocated 300,000 yuan for the promotion and development of cigarettes. I believe that flue-cured tobacco leaves are one of the fundamental raw materials for cigarettes, and I intend to propose several tens of thousands of yuan as the basic fund for curing factories. I would like to ask you to decide and send someone to supervise, so that the plans of merchants and others to improve flue-cured tobacco can be realized with the help of the government. The national economy and people's livelihood will depend on it. Whether the above is appropriate or not, please approve it and follow it. Respectfully presented to Wu, Director of the Taxation Department of the Ministry of Finance. Presented by Ding Zhenbo, Standing Committee Member of the Shanghai Tobacco Trade Association.

Repercussions of Guangdong Province's Deduction of Soybean Cake Donation 156

Chamber of Commerce Telegram: The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Southwest Political Affairs Committee yesterday, saying (brief): According to a cold telegram from the Shantou North-South Port Association and the Grain Association, Guangdong Province decided to levy a fee of 8 jiao per 100 hits on soybean cakes from the four northeastern provinces entering Guangdong, starting from the 10th of this month. The products from other provinces will still be exempted according to the original plan of April last year. However, the donation merchant Huifeng Company abruptly detained as many as 20 ships and goods, including ships and goods of Shanghai and Hankou cakes that had been sold and transported on the river surface. When asked about the order, it was said that the levy would start on the 10th, so why detain the stored goods? The order was to levy on soybean cakes from the eastern provinces, so why involve those produced in Shanghai and Hankou? They replied that it was difficult to distinguish. They thought that Shanghai and Hankou cakes were shipped from the eastern provinces. The donation merchant takes money as the main thing, turning black into white, and is unreasonable. Please provide assistance, etc. It is found that the current Guangdong Province's levy on donations of soybean cakes in the eastern provinces is scheduled to start on the 10th, which refers to those imported from May 10th. All new taxes are handled in this way. If the old stored goods are included, why set another deadline for the start of the levy? The contractor only knows to collect as much as possible, regardless of the law, and is ignorant of the overall situation. The first point that should be corrected is that it is said that Shanghai and Hankou cakes are probably shipped from the eastern provinces, which shows that the contractor does not know the business situation in various places and makes arbitrary decisions. It is even more regrettable to find that there are a total of 10 factories in Jiangsu Province that manufacture soybean cakes and peanut cakes in Shanghai, Changzhou, Wuxi, and Kunshan. There are five factories in Hankou. The origin of the raw materials is the five provinces of Shandong, Henan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangsu. The bean production in these five provinces is abundant, and the price is especially cheap. Since September 18, the import of soybean cakes from the three northeastern provinces has been subject to heavy taxes. Therefore, each factory, for the sake of cost, has absolutely no use for bean materials from the eastern provinces. The trademark of each factory's cake is being collected by the Shanghai Grain and Oil Cake Industry Association and submitted to the government offices in Guangdong Province for record. Even the goods that have been detained by the contractor have factory names and imprints that can be used as evidence and are easy to distinguish. The second point that should be corrected is that, regarding the above two requests, I implore you to quickly take charge of handling them, which is convenient for the public. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce bows,

Grain Industry Telegram: Gu Xinyi, chairman of the Shanghai Grain and Oil Cake Industry Association, previously stated that the Shantou donation merchant mistakenly recognized the soybean cakes and peanut cakes shipped to the area as products from the eastern provinces and detained them for heavy taxation. In addition to having telegraphed the authorities in Guangzhou and Shantou on the 13th to correct this, he also telegraphed the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Finance yesterday, requesting that they be ordered to release them. The content is as follows (brief): It is found that the Zhongxing steamship loaded 18,200 pieces of soybean cake and peanut cake from this factory and transported them to Guangzhou. They were mistakenly recognized by the local donation merchant Huifeng Company as goods from the eastern provinces and charged heavy taxes. At the same time, it was also reported by the guild members that the cakes shipped to Shantou on various ships are said by donation merchants to be produced in the eastern provinces and must be treated as imported fertilizer and charged heavy taxes, etc. Please immediately telegraph to prove the release. It is found that the tax collection in Guangdong Province is handled by the donation merchant Huanfeng Company. Recently, Huanfeng Company announced that it had received an order from the Commissioner of Finance of Guangdong Province to treat the soybean cake transported from the three northeastern provinces as imported fertilizer for farmland and collect a surcharge of 8 hao per 100 jin. If they are soil-made cakes not produced in the three northeastern provinces, they are not subject to taxation. Then the tax boundary is clear like stars, why is it that the ink is not dry, and suddenly the soil-made cakes at the entrance are either said to be imported from the eastern provinces, or the raw materials are produced in the eastern provinces. They even think that the trademark can be ordered directly from the factories in the eastern provinces. There are many far-fetched things, the intention is to attach to the ranks of foreign goods, and must be taxed heavily. Such strange things, Liang Yong surprised. Since September 18, the government has vigorously implemented the blockade policy, and all goods imported from the eastern provinces have been taxed as foreign goods, so imports have suddenly become rare, and domestic factories have been established to meet the needs, and they have followed one after another. If Shanghai has more than enough, Changde, Dade, Xinshui, Fengchangji, Wuxi Hengde, Runfeng, Changzhou Xiefeng, Kunshan Housheng, and Hankou factories, there are 15 factories with equipment, all self-made, sold domestically, and Guangzhou and Shantou are the most prosperous. The manufacturing raw materials are all collected from the five provinces of Shandong, Henan, Anhui, Hubei, and Jiangsu. In recent years, the bean production in these five provinces has been abundant and surplus everywhere, and the price is extremely low, so all factories take it from this. If it is as Huanfeng Company pointed out, then the import will be subject to heavy taxes, and more freight will be required, and the cost will be more expensive. I would like to ask why manufacturers bother to set up factories by themselves and put themselves in a loss? All of this is a very obvious fact. If you consider it carefully, how can you not understand? It is only because the donation merchant is responsible for the tax collection, only counting the prosperity of the tax revenue and the thickness of his own profits, and he does not care about turning black into white, and he is bound to collect the tax. Once this end is opened, the inland oil cake industry, which is still in its infancy, will be at a loss, where can we expect its development? What's more, cake is the only fertilizer for farmland. Directly taxing the factory heavily is indirectly increasing the burden on farmers. Now the rural areas are bankrupt and industry and commerce are in trouble. Above and below, we are working hard to realize the revival of the countryside and increase production. The central government implemented the blockade policy in the eastern provinces the year before last, and recently Guangdong Province added heavy taxes on imported fertilizer, all of which are good policies to protect domestic production. Guangzhou and Shantou donation merchants do not see this, only the tax is collected, and they want to eliminate the domestic production opportunities and speak for the imported fertilizer. How can the above meet the central government's intentions and how can the below comfort the people's hope? The guild feels it and is deeply frightened. In addition to having telegraphed the authorities in Guangzhou and Shantou on New Year's Day to correct it, it is reasonable to state the facts directly. I implore you to consult the Guangdong Provincial Government, and order the Commissioner of Finance to strictly order Huanfeng Company, the donation merchant in Guangzhou and Shantou, to quickly release the domestic cakes of this factory that have been detained this time, and not to arbitrarily cause trouble in the future, so as to maintain domestic products and comply with government orders.

Guo Boling Spoke at the Engineers' Association the Night Before Last; Setting up a Factory to Manufacture Oxygen Caused Foreign Merchants to Lower Prices 159

The Shanghai Branch of the Chinese Institute of Engineers held a regular meeting at the Bankers' Association Club at 7 PM on the 16th of this month. More than 20 people attended the meeting. After Chairman Xu Peihuang reported on the association's affairs, Mr. Guo Boling, a member, was invited to give a speech on the topic of "The Use of Oxygen and Its Manufacture." After Guo Jun studied in the United Kingdom and returned to China, he served as a key position in the railway, coal, iron mine, and arsenal aspects. First, he described the wide range of uses of oxygen in industry, medicine, and military affairs. Secondly, he described the various manufacturing methods of liquid oxygen in European and American countries and the advantages and disadvantages of various methods. In view of the lack of domestic factories manufacturing oxygen, it is necessary to rely on foreign merchants for supply, and the price is high. Therefore, he raised funds to establish China Refining Gas Company to manufacture oxygen, and began production last year. The quality is pure and has been certified by British and German experts. Many purchasers. Two foreign manufacturers in this city, therefore, lowered prices and dumped them. Before the company was established, the price of liquid oxygen per cubic foot was more than two yuan. After the company's products were produced, the price dropped to about eight jiao. However, Guo Jun explained that the company expected this kind of thing to happen, has strong capital, and decided to fight unremittingly. After the speech, each member asked and discussed the manufacturing technology in detail. The meeting adjourned at 10 o'clock.

The Taxpayers' Association Sends Three Letters to the Public Works Department to Correct the Cases of Water Cut-Offs, Fire Cut-Offs, and Shanty Towns 160

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association sent separate letters to Mr. Zhong Si, Director-General of the Public Works Department of the Public Concession, yesterday regarding the re-cutting of water in Peide Lane on Xinza Road, the deadline for demolishing shanty towns on Qiqihar Road, and the fact that Cai Songmao's cigarette paper shop had paid the electricity bill but had the fire meter cut off, requesting that they be investigated and handled separately. The three letters are recorded as follows:

Order to Turn on Water Immediately 161

To Whom It May Concern: According to a letter from Wang Xianyu, the lawyer stated, "According to the letter from all the tenants of Peide Lane on Xinza Road, the water supply of the tenants was cut off by the water company at the instigation of the landlord Tianzhu Church on the 24th of last month. The tenants argued in accordance with the provisions of the patent contract of March 17, 1928, and May 3, 1933, that the water company shall not listen to the landlord's request and cut off the water supply to houses where the landlord pays the water bill and the house is inhabited. The company knew that it was wrong and automatically turned on the water at 2:00 PM on the 5th of this month. Fortunately, the company regretted its past mistakes and did not repeat the tragedy. Later, on the 8th of this month, the company sent a letter saying that it was necessary to pay a deposit of 1,000 yuan for using the main water meter and sign a contract, etc. At 10:30 AM on the 10th, they followed the instructions to carry cash to the company to negotiate, and declared that this payment was purely to pay on behalf of the landlord to avoid the company's loss due to the landlord's failure to pay the fee, and that they would seek compensation from the landlord in the future. However, the company replied that this contract was paid by the tenants themselves and had nothing to do with the landlord. The tenants previously refused to install separate water meters because the landlord did not deduct the water bill in the rent. This time, the contract was signed, which was no different from admitting that there was no water bill in the landlord's rent, and it was paid by the tenants themselves. Please note on the side of the contract that the words "pay on behalf of the landlord" were also rejected. It is obvious that they are biased towards the landlord. They immediately declared that if the money was not willing to be accepted, it would be deposited in the Public Works Department and other words and withdrew. Without waiting a moment, the company sent someone in a car to close the water meter and implement the second water cut-off, repeating its inhuman approach, in order to achieve its private conspiracy to force submission. Such behavior is simply taking water cut-offs as a child's play and human life as a trifle. We specially entrust you to send a letter to the association and ask you to quickly send a letter to the Public Works Department to inform the company to restore the water immediately and stop this inhumane behavior from happening repeatedly, etc. It is found that the installation of separate water meters and the water bill are directly paid by the users. The Shanghai Real Estate Association had a notice stating that the landlord should deduct the water bill of seven and a half cents included in the rent to the tenants. Now, the landlord of Peide Lane has not deducted the water bill of seven and a half cents included in the rent to the tenants, which means that the bill for not paying the water bill has not been fulfilled in the first place, then it is still the same as the situation of bearing the payment of the water bill. According to the patent contract, the water company should not cut off the water. Now, the tenants of this lane, in order to avoid trouble for the water company, pay the deposit and bear the water bill. It is only necessary for the water company to note on the receipt, even on the water contract, that it is paid on behalf of the landlord, which is benevolence and righteousness, and it is a civil act that should be. The water company forgets its legal responsibility to obtain the franchise and rejects it and cuts off the water immediately. The statement that it is biased towards the landlord is difficult to accept. It should be requested that your office order the water company to turn on the water immediately to save the people and maintain the contract."

Do Not Demolish the Straw Sheds 162

To the esteemed Bureau,

We have recently learned that your Bureau, citing hygiene as the reason, intends to demolish around fifty straw sheds located along Qihar Road and Yanshan Road before May 21st. Our Association, in principle, has no objection to the demolition of straw sheds to improve the city's appearance and benefit public hygiene. However, on one hand, the general social and economic conditions must be taken into account, and on the other hand, the living conditions of the impoverished classes must be considered. If the reason for demolition is hygiene, improvements to sanitation facilities should simply be ordered. If demolition is ordered simply because something is considered unhygienic, then even tall buildings and magnificent mansions may also have unhygienic aspects. Would you then order their demolition? Our Association's opinion is that existing structures should be maintained and improved in terms of sanitation facilities, and that no new ones should be allowed to appear. This matter concerns the survival of the impoverished classes and the stability of society. We respectfully request your Bureau to consider this matter at length, and we would be most grateful.

Investigate the Power Cut 163

To the esteemed Bureau,

According to a letter from Cai Hequan on May 7th, he states that his merchant has been running a Cai Songmao cigarette and paper shop in Yongcheng Lane, Huaji Road, for several years, with a deposit of fifty taels of silver for the electric lights. Last Wednesday, he received a letter from the power company stating that the electricity bill was 28 yuan and 18 cents. He paid them yesterday, but since it was Sunday, he paid it this morning at 7:30 am. Unexpectedly, at 8:30 am, the company suddenly came to cut the meter, handed him a receipt on the spot, ignored it, and cut the line without permission, fleeing like a fugitive. He immediately sent his apprentice to report to the power company, but the employee said that it would cost three yuan to reconnect the line. We dare to ask your Association to quickly investigate this matter to avoid such harsh treatment and to have compassion for merchants. Our Association believes that even if electricity bills are overdue and unpaid, the electricity can be cut off. However, if the person cutting off the power sees a receipt showing that the electricity bill has been paid, they should not cut off the power. If they do cut off the power, the fault lies with the person who cut it off. This matter concerns public utilities, and we respectfully request your Bureau to investigate.

In addition to the products produced by the participating factories themselves, other products that are not from participating factories will be selected and distributed by the Shanghai China National Products Company, so all the necessary goods are very complete. In addition to the exhibits, each factory has also brought a large number of goods to sell in various places.

Scheduled Departure 168

The group is scheduled to depart on the 20th of this month. The association has specifically decided to hold a farewell meeting at the North Station at 4:00 pm on that day. The group will depart from Shanghai and is expected to arrive in Kaifeng before the 28th, and then proceed to Zhengzhou, Luoyang, Xi'an, Lanzhou, and other places. Exhibitions will be held in each place for two weeks, so the trip will take more than three months. The exhibition venues will be found by the local governments, and the venues will be divided into sixty rooms for rent to factories as temporary sales locations. The association will charge each room one hundred and fifty yuan to cover the expenses of publicity and decoration. The group has a major responsibility for promoting domestic goods in the Northwest, and the people of the Northwest will sincerely welcome them at that time.

Pleasing a Dancing Girl with Wishful Thinking - A One Yuan Savings Book Changed to a Thousand Yuan - The Wife Delighted When She Found the Savings Book, but the Truth Was Revealed by Her Uncle - Foolish Gold Bought Love, Willingly Stepping into the Criminal Net 170

Xie Jiafu, a native of Ningbo, is 22 years old and lives at No. 7, Sunjili, Rue de la Cathédrale, in the French Concession. He runs a yellow sand and gravel business. He married a woman from the same village, Le Mingzhufeng, who is the same age as Xie. The couple loved each other very much. However, Xie was young and handsome, dressed in Western suits and leather shoes, and looked like a rich young man. He was fond of romance and often frequented歌台舞榭, song and dance venues. Recently, he met a dancing girl named Xue Fengzhu. In order to gain the trust of Miss Xue and to increase their love, Xie had a whimsical idea. On the afternoon of the 24th of last month, at 2:00 pm, he went to the Fuxu Road Branch of the China Industrial Bank at No. 517 and paid one yuan to open a savings account. He used Xue Fengzhu's name to deposit the money, and the bank issued him a savings book with number 394, which Xie took home. Unexpectedly, Xie then

Indulged in Wishful Thinking 171

The next day, he added the words "nine hundred and ninety-nine yuan" himself in the book, affixed a fake seal, and made it up to a thousand yuan. After completing this procedure, he placed the book in his suitcase, waiting for the opportunity to show it to Miss Xue, in order to boast of his wealth and that he had deposited a thousand yuan for her, as a false pretense to increase their love. However, Xie's wife, Le, because she had long known that her husband was seeking pleasure outside and had met a dancing girl, could not help but be jealous, so she often took the opportunity to search Xie's pockets and had obtained letters and photos of Miss Xue, advising her husband to no avail. On the evening of the 10th of this month, when her husband went out, she searched her husband's suitcase under the bed and found this bank savings book.

Secretly Pleased 172

She thought that her husband still had some private money left and had deposited it in the bank. However, because she was illiterate and did not know the amount of money in the book, she gave the book to her brother, Le Jiafu (28 years old, who runs a construction factory), who lived with her. After reading it, he learned that the book belonged to her husband's mistress, the dancing girl Xue Fengzhu. This made her even more jealous. The next day, she asked her brother Le Jiafu to take the book to the China Industrial Bank branch to inquire. Le took the book to the bank to check, and wanted to withdraw three hundred yuan. After the teller checked the account book, he found that there was only one yuan in Xue Fengzhu's account. Where did the added nine hundred and ninety-nine yuan come from?

Joining Together for a Thousand Yuan 173

The money was obviously a fraudulent alteration of the savings book. He immediately reported to the bank manager Zhu Xuefan and reported to the French police. Detective Superintendent Jin Jiulin, along with detective Yang Yilong, immediately rushed to arrest Le. After interrogation, they also arrested Xie Jiafu and Xie Le. After questioning, the report was made to the head of the police, who ordered them to be detained and sent to the Second Special District Court for further investigation. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Li Changnian of the Second Special Court interrogated them in the Criminal Court. Yao Zhaodi, the police lawyer, stated the police investigation process and presented the altered savings book as evidence. He filed a lawsuit against the three defendants for forgery of seals under Articles 224, 234, and 363 of the Criminal Law.

Attempted Fraud 174

The plaintiff, Zhu Xuefan, was represented by the bank employee Zhang Binghai, who stated that the defendant Le Jiafu brought the book to the bank, checked the deposit, and requested to withdraw three hundred yuan. When questioned, Le Jiafu confessed that his sister had entrusted him to take the book to the China Industrial Bank branch to inquire about the deposit, and he did not dare to request a withdrawal or commit fraud. Xie Jiafu confessed that he went to the Industrial Bank branch to open a savings account and filled out the savings book himself. He did it to please the dancing girl and make his wife angry, and had no other intentions. Le confessed that she obtained the book from her husband's suitcase, knew it was the dancing girl's deposit, and asked her brother to take it to inquire, but she did not tell her brother to withdraw the deposit. Then, the police clerk and the defendant's lawyer argued with each other. The court ordered the end of the debate and scheduled the verdict.

A Murder Occurs in a Rent Arrears Closure Case - Swallowing Smoke and Spitting Mist, Hearing the Police Knocking on the Door - Wang Fugen Fell and Died 177

The Xu family at No. 6, Lane 167, Beihai Road, was sued for rent arrears and the First Special Court approved a provisional attachment. On the 14th of this month, the request was granted. At around 2:00 pm, the court sent judicial police to seal the house. Unexpectedly, Wang Fugen, 34 years old, was lying on a couch in the house, smoking opium. Suddenly, he heard the police knocking on the door urgently, thinking they were coming to arrest him. He immediately ran to the drying platform, intending to escape to the neighbor's house to hide. Unexpectedly, he was careless and fell to the ground, suffering serious head injuries. After the police reported to the Old Gate Police Station and ordered detectives to investigate, he was taken to the hospital for treatment to no avail. He died the day before yesterday. The body was taken to the Feilun Road Morgue. Yesterday, the Procuratorate of the First Special Court appointed Prosecutor Guo Wei, along with forensic doctor Zhang Yan and clerk Wang Zuyi, to go to the morgue to examine the body. After inquiring about the situation from the judicial police chief who went to seal the door that day, Mr. Guo concluded that the deceased Wang Fugen died from head injuries sustained in a fall. The body was handed over to his wife, Wang Chen, who signed a guarantee to take it back for burial.

Shanghai South: Public Bus Routes - Steps Defined by the Municipal Public Works Bureau 180

The Municipal Public Works Bureau, recognizing that public transportation in Shanghai South has been greatly inconvenienced since the former Shanghai South Automobile Company, which was run by merchants, failed due to poor management and ceased operations, presented a request to the municipal government last October to have the Bureau continue to operate the public bus service in order to develop transportation in Shanghai South. After several months of preparation, the Bureau purchased vehicles and established a Public Bus Management Office, which began operations on April 1 of this year. However, the Bureau was very cautious about how to define the routes for the public buses. After careful consideration and weighing the urgency, it was decided to first operate routes two and three of the former Shanghai South Public Bus Company. The previous route two, from Old West Gate to Longhua Line, was renamed route one to accommodate citizens traveling to Longhua for sightseeing and to meet the needs of residents in that area. Route three, the circular route around the city, remains route three. Although this line is already served by trams, there are many passengers, and the Chinese Tram Company has entered into a contract with the French Tram Company to operate only eight trams each, and neither company is allowed to freely increase the number of trams. This has resulted in extremely crowded passengers, which is not appropriate. In order to meet the needs of citizens, it is necessary to add trams to this route for adjustment. Moreover, the transportation business has a close relationship with the municipal government. The more transportation tools there are, the faster the city will prosper. It is not only possible to alleviate the crowding of passengers. However, the Bureau's current two public bus routes are only the beginning of the city-run public buses. Other routes in the Shanghai South area are also being tested and prepared for expansion at any time, so that the transportation network of the city can be connected and contribute to the construction of Greater Shanghai.

Tao Jia Yao Sues Gao Xiaochen for Assault - Gao Denies Assaulting Tao - Court Orders Forensic Examination 190

Previously, Gao Xiaochen had filed a private prosecution against Tao Jia Yao in the Second Special District Court for fraud. During the court hearing on the third of this month, both parties were ordered to go outside and reconcile. After leaving the courtroom, Tao Jia Yao was suddenly attacked and vomited blood near the stairwell. This matter has already been reported in the previous newspaper. Now, Tao has retained Luo Jiaheng, Wang Zaoshi, and Li Guozhen, three lawyers, to file a private prosecution with the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court, accusing Gao Xiaochen of assault. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Fanglian summoned Gao to the Second Criminal Court. The plaintiff, due to serious injuries, was unable to appear in court and was represented by his lawyers who stated the grounds for the prosecution. They stated that after the court adjourned on the third of this month, when Tao Jia Yao was walking to the stairs, the defendant Gao Xiaochen suddenly shouted loudly at Tao, "I must beat you to death!" After saying this, he punched Tao hard from behind. Fortunately, two bailiffs saw it and stopped him, and helped Tao into the lawyers' lounge. At that time, Tao vomited two mouthfuls of blood due to the injury. Judge Xiong witnessed this and ordered the clerk to take notes. He also reopened the court, summoned Gao to the court, and reprimanded him for the assault, immediately ordering him to post bail (which his representative lawyer did). He also instructed Tao Jia Yao to go to the forensic office for an injury examination and file another lawsuit. Because it was late and past office hours, the forensic doctor had already gone home. Therefore, Tao went home and immediately asked Dr. Song Yuqi of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to come to his home for treatment. Now there is a medical certificate to prove this. Unexpectedly, Tao cannot sleep at night and cannot eat, and his condition has suddenly worsened. Yesterday, he vomited blood again (now the phlegm sample can be brought to court as evidence). It is found that the defendant Gao Xiaochen is a former military officer and skilled in boxing. Considering the nature of the assault, it is requested that the severity of future injuries be reserved, and that the defendant be punished according to Article 295, Section 2 of the Criminal Law, for the corresponding crime, etc. In response to the interrogation, the defendant Gao Xiaochen stated, "Tao Jia Yao and I were originally friends. A lawsuit arose due to debt matters. Because he said unpleasant things about me in court, after the court adjourned, I was walking outside and called Tao to stop to reason with him. Because he didn't hear me, I stepped forward and grabbed his clothes, but I did not hit him. Tao Jia Yao has a long-standing illness. When he was in the sanatorium, I went to the hospital to visit him," etc. Lawyers Xiang Xun and Liu Cailiang defended him. Bailiff Xu Huizhang, No. 529, testified, "On the third of this month, I was on duty upstairs. When the court adjourned, Tao Jia Yao was walking in front, and I was behind Tao, and Gao Xiaochen was behind me. At that time, Gao angrily said to Tao, 'You shouldn't have said I was poor in court!' At the same time, he stepped forward and grabbed Tao's right arm. I was afraid that something would happen, so I immediately shouted to stop him and sent Tao into the lawyers' lounge." The judge asked if he saw Tao vomit blood, and he replied, "I saw Tao vomit two mouthfuls of blood at the time." Witness Cai Ying testified, "I work in the lawyers' lounge. I didn't see the dispute when both sides were arguing, but when Tao arrived at the lawyers' lounge, I saw Tao vomit blood." At this point, lawyer Luo Jiaheng stated that Tao Jia Yao had been to court several times, each time for three or four hours, and had never vomited blood. How could he have a long-standing illness? Judge Wu ordered a forensic doctor to be dispatched to Tao's home along with both parties' lawyers to examine the plaintiff's injuries for verification.

Meeting of the Executive Committee of the Postal Workers Union 193

The Shanghai Postal Workers Union held its 42nd Executive Committee meeting on May 16th. Chairman Shui Xiangyun presided. (A) Formalities. (B) Matters Reported. (1) Letter from the Shanghai Postmaster: "Regarding your request to resume the qualification examination, special approval is granted to hold it in May of this year. Instructed to inform." (2) Report of the Standing Committee. (A) Regarding the request of messenger members to participate in this postal worker qualification examination, after consultation with the bureau, due to regulations, only postal assistants are allowed to participate in this examination. The request could not be processed and the situation has been explained to the members. (B) The union requested that all employees, regardless of rank, be issued badges. According to the Postmaster's reply, the General Post Office instructed that in addition to postal assistants and above being issued badges, messengers and laborers would be issued chest badges or armbands when necessary. The union maintains its original request for everyone to be issued badges. After negotiation with the bureau, they agreed to investigate with other agencies before proceeding. (3) Standing Committee member Zhang Kechang reported that he went to Beijing on the 13th of this month to attend the General Assembly Standing Committee meeting. He earnestly stated the important pending issues to the Central Party Headquarters, the Legislative Yuan, the Ministry of Communications, and the National Aviation Construction Association. The results are briefly reported below. (A) Postal Workers Aircraft - After requesting the Aviation Construction Association to purchase it as soon as possible, the Association agreed to wait for the General Assembly to submit a formal submission before discussing the purchase and naming of the aircraft. (B) Regarding the issue of combined postal and telecommunications services, the committee members specifically explained to Vice Minister Zhang of the Ministry of Communications the impact of the combination on postal economics and administration. Vice Minister Zhang stated that the combination is completely different from a merger. The combination of postal and telecommunications services is based on the principle of saving expenses and facilitating the public. It will not disrupt the economics and administration of both parties. He hoped postal workers would not worry too much. During the trial period, if facts occur that violate the above two principles, the Ministry will give full consideration to the opinions of subordinates and seek special solutions. (C) Resuming the personnel qualification examination system - Vice Minister Zhang sincerely expressed his support for this matter and intended to instruct the General Office to work with the General Assembly to design and implement it effectively. (D) Recruitment of students to study in Austria - The union and the General Assembly have repeatedly suggested methods. Vice Minister Zhang did not express a definite opinion on this, but hoped postal workers would not misunderstand. (E) Regarding the consolidation of the postal base implementation plan, the situation of reviewing regulations was inquired at the Legislative Yuan, and opinions on this matter were expressed. Legislative Yuan Secretary-General Liang Hancao agreed to accept it and forward it to the Regulations and Economics Committees for prompt action. (F) Recently, the Ministry of Communications recruited accounting personnel for affiliated agencies. According to Vice Minister Zhang, the postal accounting system and existing accounting personnel are all good. The personnel recruited this time will be assigned to telecommunications agencies in the future. (4) At noon on the 12th of this month, the union and the labor union jointly hosted a banquet at Xinghua Restaurant for Vice Minister Yu Feipeng of the Ministry of Communications and Director Wei Yifu of the Postal Administration to bid farewell to their departure for overseas inspection. (C) Matters for Discussion. (1) The Postal Workers' Hospital Preparatory Committee submitted a proposal, based on the joint meeting of the two associations, recommending that the authorities establish a Postal Workers' Hospital to promote the welfare of postal workers. Is this feasible? Please discuss the proposal. Resolution: The two associations will jointly send a letter to the authorities for approval. (2) The 17th Branch submitted a request from member Qian Zengming et al. to request the authorities to negotiate for the assignment of replacement personnel to cover those on leave and to require that appropriate meal allowances be paid for overtime work to ensure equality. How should this be handled? Please discuss the proposal. Resolution: Forwarded to the Negotiation Department for investigation. (3) Members Yang Zong et al. of the 11th Branch submitted a proposal stating that they were all accepted in the 1931 postal worker examination but were rejected by the General Office. They have petitioned for negotiation without success and now earnestly request transfer to the bureau for negotiation to approve their employment as postal workers without examination. Resolution: Handled by the Standing Committee. (4) The Medical Department submitted a proposal stating that member Qian Qisheng accused the public Shanghai Hospital of not providing emergency room service at night. Fatal Beating Over Gambling 194

Wang Qishan, age twenty-one, from Funing, lived in a shed on Datong Road in Zhabei. He earned his living by pulling a rickshaw. Last night around eight o'clock, he and Zhou Xuegao, also from Funing, who worked as a handyman on Shunxing Road at the end of Datong Road, gathered to play a card game. Unexpectedly, Wang and Zhou suddenly got into an argument over a minor matter and started fighting each other. Wang Qishan was no match for Zhou Xuegao and was knocked down. Although others tried to mediate, Zhou continued to beat Wang, hitting a vital point. Wang immediately lost consciousness and died. Zhou, realizing he had caused a disaster, immediately turned to flee, but was stopped by fellow gamblers. They summoned the police from the Sun Temple Fourth District Police Station, who arrested the assailant and took him, along with the gambling equipment and witnesses, to the Fourth District Headquarters. After questioning by the District Chief, he was ordered to be temporarily detained pending referral to the Judicial Section for further interrogation this morning due to the case involving a death. He also ordered the local bailiff to report to the court and request an inquest.

Reading Q&A

Review of Several Basic Problems in Philosophy (III) 206

Having explained the content of "identity" and "unity" for several days, today we will further explain the two questions, "two" and "three," raised by Mr. Sheng. Editor

Two: 'The identity of opposites is relative, the struggle of opposites is absolute'

This is the most important and most fundamental part of the epistemology of dialectics. Within the large group of dialectical materialists, there are many theorists and practitioners who, due to incorrect understanding or insufficient knowledge of this fundamental part, unknowingly find themselves in a situation of struggling with dialectics. For example, Bogdanov, Deborin, Lóvol, and Bukharin. The general theorists of the Second International, led by Kautsky, also regarded the identity of opposites as absolute and as a permanent harmony, obliterating the absoluteness of the struggle of opposites, and thus becoming traitors to the revolution. From this, we can know the importance of this principle.

So, how should we interpret the phrase "the identity of opposites is relative"? Let's still use the examples we used before. Yellow cattle and water buffalo are two opposing objects, they have similarities, they both have horns, they both eat grass, they both ruminate, and they can both plow fields and pull carts, which is called the identity of opposites. But this kind of identity is not absolute, that is to say, yellow cattle are not completely equal to water buffalo. Because their fur color and personality have various differences, so it is relative (conditional). The same is true for all natural objects such as horses and mules. Since the development of natural science, it has increasingly proved the correctness of this principle. For example, when water is exposed to sunlight, it evaporates into gas and becomes clouds. When clouds encounter cold, they turn into rain and revert to water. Also, such as positive and negative numbers, differential and integral calculus in mathematics. Astronomy and geography, physics and chemistry, all have commonalities, but none are absolute. These are examples from natural science.

If we talk about social, political, and economic science, the reader will understand it more clearly. For example, during the French Revolution, the bourgeoisie, the proletariat, and the peasant petty bourgeoisie jointly opposed the autocratic regime of landlords and feudal aristocrats, and demanded democratic republic. This illustrates that the interests of each opposing class are the same in the democratic revolution against landlords and feudal aristocrats, and the identity of these opposing classes – mainly the bourgeoisie and the proletariat! – is only a temporary identity in the (conditional) revolution against feudal autocracy, not a permanent identity, not an absolute identity. The failure of the "Paris Commune," the great bloodshed of workers and peasants, and the "Jacobin" regime are all concrete facts illustrating this principle, that is, the example of the February Revolution in Russia in 1917 mentioned earlier, also illustrates "the struggle of opposites is absolute." As long as we pay a little attention to social phenomena, we can find extremely appropriate examples anytime, anywhere.

In short, there is nothing permanent and unchanging. For example, water turns into clouds, wood and bamboo stems turn into paper, chicken eggs hatch into chicks, and seeds germinate, grow branches and leaves, bloom and bear fruit, and then turn into seeds again; anytime, anywhere, one form changes into another form; this changing process turns into its own opposite. The immobility of any process is relative. But the transformation of one process into another process is absolute. Therefore, it is said that "the identity of opposites! Condensation, harmony, and balance! are conditional, temporary, transient, and relative. The struggle of mutually exclusive opposites is absolute, the same as development and movement is absolute.”

Only by grasping this correct law of cognition can people grasp the key to the self-movement of all existing things; only it can provide the key to understanding change, development, sudden change, gradual interruption, transformation into opposites, the disappearance of the old and the growth of the new. Otherwise, the world will be seen as static, dead, and lifeless. (III) "Human knowledge is an active process that is included as a motive in multi-faceted social practice."

As mentioned before, nature, society, thought, forms, and concepts are separate unity and unified division; all are inseparable from the laws of contradiction, change, development, old decrease, and new birth, so human knowledge is not static and dead, but lively and vivid.

With the invention and development of natural science, human knowledge of natural phenomena has greatly improved. Before Darwin's theory of evolution was invented, it was thought that humans were created by God. Later, human knowledge of humans denied the divine creation of God and affirmed that humans, like other creatures, were transformed from other animals, that is, transformed from apes. Columbus's successful navigation discovered a new world – the Americas – outside the old world. Magellan's successful circumnavigation discovered that the Earth is round and denied the previous understanding that the Earth is square. The invention of astronomy and the successful manufacturing of various astronomical instruments denied the previous recognition of eight planets and established the existence of nine planets. The lunar and solar eclipses that people thought were magical have also become unremarkable due to the development of astronomy. The invention of electrons denied the assumption that atoms were the highest element, and the invention of machines eliminated small-scale industrial workshops. The invention of the fire plow and harvester created new-style large farms.

In the late 18th century and mid-19th century, the development of history and social sciences confirmed the theory of inevitable social change. Primitive communist society transformed into tribal society; tribal society transformed into feudal society; feudal society transformed into capitalist society, and capitalist society will also decline and transform into another kind of society (socialist society). The process of transformation may be fast or slow, or the forms may be different, but the recognition of transformation is certain.

When European capitalist forces invaded China, it shook the rural economies of various provinces in southern China – especially the coastal provinces such as Guangdong, Fujian, Zhejiang, and Jiangsu. British machine-woven cloth shattered the large cloth of Nanjing and the native cloth of Guangzhou; it also shattered the textile industry of rural housewives. At first, people only thought that the "red-haired people" were bad, competing with Chinese people for food, and foreign machines were bad, taking away the jobs of the handicraft industry. Therefore, the farmers of Sanyuanjing in Guangzhou (a rural area on the outskirts of Guangzhou, with textiles as the economic life of the entire village, with a population of more than 30,000) went to Guangzhou in groups to protest and smashed foreign commercial houses and their machines. The demolition of the newly built Shanghai-Wusong Railway also had the same anti-foreign and machine-hating significance as the Sanyuanjing farmers' riots. This kind of thing also happened in England when the machine industry gradually developed, with farmers and handicraftsmen destroying machines. Later, the development of facts made people realize that this was not a question of Chinese and foreigners, machines and handicrafts, but the course of capitalist development, and the Opium War, the Sino-Japanese War, and the Boxer Rebellion, until the "May Thirtieth" Movement, the slogan of "Down with Imperialism" was recognized by people.

Because reality is changing and developing, our understanding of reality also changes with it. From the above explanation, it can be clearly seen. However, we should not think that this kind of understanding is like a mirror reflecting a person's face, reflecting it without any difference or conditions. For example, (anti-imperialism). It is not because we already have the fact of anti-imperialism that we reflect the slogan of "anti-imperialism". Rather, it is because the imperialist aggression is intensifying and the national crisis is deepening, that we regard the slogan of "anti-imperialism" as a fighting banner that can liberate the Chinese nation in practice (in the movement). Another example is "resistance to Japan". It is not because there are activities of volunteer soldiers and the Battle of Shanghai that the understanding of resistance to Japan is reflected. Rather, it is after the "September 18th" Incident that Japanese imperialism has been approaching step by step, and it is recognized from practice that resistance to Japan is the task of resolving the most urgent crisis at present. If understanding is regarded as a reflection of change, then the slogans of "anti-imperialism" and "resistance to Japan" are just soulless dead slogans. The May Thirtieth Movement is only the starting point of the Chinese anti-imperialist movement becoming a conscious movement, because it put forward the slogan of anti-imperialism and popularized the anti-imperialist movement in practical movement. This is a very clear example. Readers who want to gain a thorough understanding must find examples from their own practical life. There is also a principle explanation in Chapter 2 of this book. Readers can gain a considerable understanding by reading it a few more times. (To be continued)

Athletes from the Dutch East Indies Are Scheduled to Return Home on the 19th 219

(Japan United Press Manila 17th) Athletes from the Dutch East Indies are scheduled to depart for their country on the 19th, the day the conference closes. However, because it rained today and was extended by one day, they are considering whether to postpone their departure. However, there will not be a ship returning to the country until one month after the 19th, so it was decided to depart for home on the scheduled date regardless of whether the conference closes or not.

Referee Error Japan Protests 220

High Hurdles and Fifty Meter Freestyle

(Dentsu News Agency 17th) In the high hurdles preliminary, Adachi Kiyoshi (Japan), who was announced as the third qualifier in Group B, was disqualified for knocking down three hurdles. It has now been announced that Shimizu Kotaro (Japan), who was fourth, has qualified. Shimizu and Garcia (Philippines), who was first, crossed the last hurdle side by side, and slipped and fell due to his feet, resulting in fourth place. He is expected to be active in the final.

(Dentsu News Agency Manila 17th) In last night's 50-meter freestyle preliminary, Japanese athlete Takahashi won second place, but the referee mistakenly judged him to have failed to qualify. Therefore, the Japanese side today filed a written protest with the headquarters of this association at noon, requesting a rematch. The protest has been submitted to Mr. Hirana, so the conference immediately convened a conference competition committee at the conference headquarters to discuss.

(Dentsu News Agency Manila 17th) As reported in the previous telegram, the Japanese athlete Adachi Kiyoshi in the high hurdles preliminary was disqualified for knocking down three hurdles, and Shimizu Kotaro was promoted to third place. On the 17th, the Philippine Association reversed the previous judgment, announced that Adachi had qualified, and canceled Shimizu as the third. Therefore, the Japanese side was very angry at the Philippine side's indecision and lodged a serious protest. The Philippine side said that Shimizu had violated other people's routes when he fell, so he was disqualified. As a result, a dispute occurred, but the result was that Japan's protest was accepted, and it was decided that Shimizu would qualify. On the other hand, there has been no response to the issue of swimmer Takahashi (Japan) in the 50-meter preliminary. Philippine Sports Association Director Hirana said that the swimming staff competition committee recognized Takahashi's right to attend the final and decided to have seven people compete in the final. The official reply will be given on the 18th. In addition, the Philippine side's approval or disapproval of Japan's proposal regarding future refereeing methods must be answered in writing, so there is a lot of criticism from all parties for the Philippine side's repeated misjudgments.
