The Grand Arrival of Our Delegation in the Philippines Tens of Thousands of Overseas Chinese Men and Women Welcome Them in the City Li Huitang and Yang Xiuqiong Attracted the Most Attention 丨Sent by Yan Wenchun, Our Newspaper's Special Correspondent in Manila丨 222

On the 8th of this month, our election group arrived in Manila on the President McKinley ship of the Dalian Company, which almost shook the entire overseas Chinese community in Manila, so the welcome was worth recording.

(1) The Reception Committee is Busy with Preparations

For social organizations that wanted to join the welcoming party with motorcycles, the committee pre-made hundreds of paper signs and hundreds of small national flags. Each car could receive two paper signs and two small national flags, so two people were specially assigned to distribute the flags and signs the day before yesterday, which was very busy.

(2) President McKinley's Ship Arrived Late

President McKinley's ship did not arrive at the port until 9:50. The chairman of the Chinese Chamber of Commerce and Secretary Liu Xuesong first took a customs launch out of the dike to board the ship to welcome them. It is estimated that more than 200 cars were prepared by various overseas Chinese organizations and individuals to go to the pier on this day. The Wang family's Taoyuan Hall of the Self-Government Association prepared ten cars. In addition, the Philippine Sports Association prepared twenty large and small cars to specially transport the athletes, doing their best as hosts. After 8 o'clock, nearly 10,000 overseas Chinese men and women voluntarily joined in. Pier No. 7 was so crowded that it was almost impenetrable. When the ship approached the pier, two military bands prepared by the Philippine Sports Association and the military band of the 236th Regiment of the Chinese Boy Scouts played the welcome song together. For a time, the applause was as loud as thunder.

(3) Order of the Overseas Chinese Welcoming Party

When the music was playing, the Blue Sky, White Sun, and Red Earth national emblem and the blue flag emblem presented by the Chinese Sports Association and Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng were flying in the ship. General Representative Wang Zhengting and his wife stood under the flag to receive the welcome from the overseas Chinese. The Philippine Miss (overseas Chinese woman) of this year's Carnival led 32 overseas Chinese ladies to present flowers to the general representative and female athletes. Students from the First Overseas Chinese Girls' School then sang the national anthem. While the military music was playing, Wang led the athletes off the ship and out of Pier No. 7, and immediately sat in the car prepared by Philippine Senate President Quezon. Because Quezon had just returned to the Philippines from the United States and was recuperating in Baguio, he specially sent a representative to prepare a car to welcome them to Manila. The rest of the cars followed one after another, first introduced by the chairman of the welcoming committee to the Municipal Bureau to make some courtesy with the mayor. In fact, the mayor also went to the pier to welcome them in person. Then they went to the Governor's Palace to visit the Philippine Governor, and then paraded through the major streets to La Salle College to temporarily unload their luggage and rest. It was already 12 o'clock noon.

Welcome Group of the First Overseas Chinese Girls' School

(4) Miss Mermaid Shows Greatly Surrounded 223

Miss Yang Hsiu-chiung, who won the national women's swimming championship, is known to almost all overseas Chinese women and children. Therefore, when she disembarked, she was greatly surrounded by the audience. Even Filipinos admire her beautiful figure and she is truly worthy of being called the "Mermaid of the Orient." According to Miss Yang's conversation with reporters, this is her first time to the Philippines, and she feels that the weather here is hot, even more so than in South China. Furthermore, the "ball-monster" Li Hui-tang has been to the Philippines seven or eight times. There may be some in the overseas Chinese community who do not know Wang Cheng-ting, but there are hardly any who do not know Li Hui-tang. Therefore, those who wanted to see his demeanor were also eagerly awaiting. Fortunately, Mr. Li is still energetic as ever, so physical educators are celebrating the future of Chinese football. According to Mr. Li, this time, because many great players like Tai Lin-ching could not come together, there will inevitably be some deficiencies in strength. However, the players in the football team are mainly from South China, and they will be able to handle communication more easily. Therefore, there is a great chance of winning in football.

(5) Mr. Wang's Talk with Reporters

Generally speaking, when an important person arrives, newspaper reporters regard it as an excellent source of information, so they inevitably surround them and engage in conversation. Moreover, with the recent bad news from the motherland, the overseas Chinese community wants to know accurate news even more. Mr. Wang is also an outstanding diplomat of more than ten years, so his words are even more important. The most important questions and answers are recorded below:

(Question) This time, Japan wanted to forcibly include its puppet state of "Manchukuo" in the Far Eastern Games, but our side opposed it. Due to the rules of the association, Japan reluctantly participated as before. At this session of the Far Eastern Games, a proposal to amend the constitution will be made at the regular meeting of the Far Eastern Games, and amendments will be implemented with a two-thirds majority vote. The meeting period of the standing committee happens to be within the period of the Far Eastern Games. If Japan achieves its goal, how will we deal with it? Will we immediately withdraw from the competition, or will we end on a "happy" note? (Answer) Our country has always opposed Japan's forced inclusion of the puppet "Manchukuo"... and we have never approved of it. When the Japanese representative Yamamoto Tadaoki arrived in Shanghai that day, he made this request, but I refuted him with one sentence. I asked Yamamoto, where is Manchukuo? I really don't know where Manchukuo is, how can I vote? For example, if we talk about Mr. Zheng, I should first know where Mr. Zheng is from and when he was born before I can discuss Mr. Zheng's affairs. This is very clear, so there is no need to elaborate. (Question) China and the Philippines have close relations, and the Philippines is about to become independent. It is said that Mr. Wang's visit to the Philippines this time, in addition to leading the Chinese team to participate in the Far Eastern Games and attending the Far Eastern Games Standing Committee, also has other missions, such as discussing trade and other diplomatic matters with the Philippine authorities. Is that correct? (Answer) The relationship between China and the Philippines is indeed close, but it will take at least fifteen years for the Philippines to achieve independence. It seems too early to talk about trade or other diplomatic matters at this time. Continuing, this time is just preparation. I and Philippine Senate President Quezon are old friends of many years and are like-minded. We can talk about everything with each other, but it is discussed in private friendship, not formal negotiations. (Question) When Quezon returned to Manila via Shanghai, the doctor hosted a banquet and discussed what issues? (Answer) We did not discuss any issues, it was just a reception. (Question) Japanese Ambassador to China Arima Akira recently went to Nanjing to meet with Wang Jingwei and Huang Fu to discuss Sino-Japanese affairs. Afterwards, they went to Shanghai for consultations, and then the Japanese ambassador returned to Japan to report. Is there already certainty about the opening of traffic in North China? (Answer) This matter is not very clear. (Question) The Japanese said that the Tanggu Agreement stipulates the opening of traffic between North China and the puppet state. Is that correct? (Answer) Absolutely not. (Question) Have you seen the Tanggu Agreement, Doctor? (Answer) I have seen it. (Question) Then what is the content? (Answer) The same as what is published in the newspapers. (Question) After Japan issued a new declaration on its policy towards China, it aroused reactions from European and American countries. The National Government has issued two declarations of opposition. Has this matter ended? (Answer) There is still much that can be done, the key is how to do it. I think Wang Jingwei is an important figure in the party and the country, and he will definitely not be willing to lose China's sovereignty. We should cooperate with him so that he can concentrate on serving the country. Even Mr. Chiang is not someone who would cede sovereignty and humiliate the country. (Question) It is said that Wang Jingwei recently invited the doctor to Beijing and will ask the doctor to reassume the post of Minister of Foreign Affairs. Is this true? (Answer) This is not true. (Question) You recently went to Peiping and heard that the situation there is very dangerous. Is that correct? (Answer) There is no such thing as dangerous or not dangerous. The situation in China is dangerous, not just in North China. Isn't South China the same? If the Japanese land in Guangdong with 20,000 or 30,000 heavy troops, can we resist them? At this point, the reporters saw that Mr. Wang was coughing frequently and looked very tired. Not wanting to disturb him further, they bid farewell and left.

General Description of the Situation of Various Championships The Philippines Has Already Won the Volleyball Championship Our Country Still Has Little Hope for Basketball 224

Yesterday was the sixth day of the 10th Far Eastern Games. Unfortunately, the weather was not good, and it rained heavily all day. All competitions were suspended, causing track and field, swimming, etc. to be unable to end as scheduled. The conference had no choice but to extend it by one day. Although the various championships have not yet reached the end, the situation has been determined and the clues are already there. A general description is as follows:

Football 225

Since our country drew with Japan three to three in the last session and shared the championship, the people were very indignant. In this session, we must win. In the first match against the Philippines, we won two to zero, but it felt very difficult. It was thought that the match against the newly joined strong team of the Dutch East Indies would not be optimistic, and everyone had doubts. During this period of doubt, the Dutch East Indies defeated Japan seven to one, thinking that the Dutch East Indies was avenging our country, which made people very happy. On the one hand, it also made people very apprehensive, because with such a score, even our country would feel that there was more danger than good luck. Unexpectedly, our army also won the second match against the Dutch East Indies with two to zero. Thus, fear turned into optimism. It is assumed that the mediocre Japanese army will not be our opponent. However, in the match between Japan and the Philippines, although the Philippines took the lead with three to one in the first half, Japan scored three goals in the second half, and the situation changed. The Philippine army still lost. The Japanese army's endurance and fighting spirit should not be underestimated. Our army still cannot rest easy. We only hope for a draw, then the championship will also be ours.

Basketball 226

Our country's hopes for the basketball team were not strong. Judging from the two losses to Japan in the last session and the fact that Japan also defeated the Philippines once, it is natural that the hope of winning this time is even slimmer. Before the team went abroad, the encouragement of public opinion made the players realize that they must avenge their previous defeats. Sure enough, in the first match, they defeated Japan forty-two to twenty-six. After that, the Philippine army also defeated the short army with fifty-one to thirty-five. Seeing this score, the hopes of our army increased sharply. When the time for the first match between China and the Philippines arrived, enthusiastic people in the country were all waiting with bated breath. When the telegram arrived in Shanghai, in the first half, our army lost to the Philippine army by a large margin of twelve to twenty-six. In the second half, because of the heavy rain, our side requested to stop the game, but the referee did not agree and instead ruled that our team had forfeited. The referee's unreasonable pressure was unbearable, so we protested. After deliberation by the competition committee, it was decided to overturn the referee's decision and reschedule the game for the 20th. However, looking at the situation of the second match between China and Japan, our army was fortunate to rely on Wang Yuzeng's throw in the last ten seconds to defeat Japan again with forty-eight to forty-seven. It was indeed not without a surplus of energy. Without Mr. Wang's goal, wouldn't we have lost to the Japanese army with forty-six to forty-seven? Seeing this, although we defeated Japan and avenged our previous defeats, the basketball championship, which the Philippines regards as a forbidden fruit, is probably not our country's business.

Volleyball 227

Everyone thought that volleyball, which had the most confidence in retaining the championship, was not only defeated by the Philippines, but was also eaten up by Japan, opening up an unprecedented disastrous defeat for Chinese volleyball in the history of the Far Eastern Games. It was shocking and disheartening. The Philippines first defeated Japan three to one, and our country defeated Japan three to two. Based on this calculation, our country should only be an enemy of the Philippines. However, how could we know that we would lose to the Philippines in a straight three? And how could we expect that in the second match between China and Japan, Japan would avenge us with three to one? In the second match between Japan and the Philippines, the Philippines won again with three to one. Thus, the Philippine team has three wins in three matches. In the last match against our country, no matter how we win or lose, the championship has already become the Philippine team's possession.

Tennis 228

Our country's defeat in tennis is an inevitable situation. The prior expectation that we could hope to win the championship again after the eighth session was just a nervous and overly confident idea. It should be known that the level of tennis between China and Japan is far apart. Although their first- and second-rate players go to Europe to attend the Davis Cup and other international competitions, their third- and fourth-rate players are enough to defeat our country's first-rate talents with plenty to spare. If Japan does not send out reserve members Jou Shou-chiao and Yamada, how can Hsu Cheng-shen even be able to compete for a ray of glory? Sato Hyosuke, who was defeated by our country's Lin Pao-hua and Chiu Fei-hai at the eighth Far Eastern Games in Shanghai, now that he has reunited with Mr. Chiu, Sato was quite afraid of Chiu Fei-hai before the game. But when the game started, Sato was very disappointed, unexpectedly Chiu's skills had deteriorated so much. The Chiu Fei-hai after seven years is still the same as before. Sato's disappointment is actually laughing at the Chinese players for being too depressed. We really have nothing to comfort ourselves with. As for the situation of the finals between Japan and the Philippines, Japan's Sato again won all two singles matches. Even if Yamada loses all matches, Japan will definitely win the doubles, and the championship will be stably won by Japan.

Baseball 229

Our country's baseball is just to go through the motions. It is enough to have a good performance. The Philippines this time restored players from the league, which was always considered professional, to amateur status and participated, and their strength increased sharply. And in view of the consecutive defeats to our country in the previous two sessions (our country was represented by overseas Chinese from Honolulu) and falling to third place, they vowed to avenge their shame. Judging from the strength of the Philippine team in this session, there is indeed a possibility of winning the championship. Japan is also left behind. In the first match between our country and the Philippines, the Philippines won with twenty-five to one. The Philippines got fifteen hits, and our country also got seven, but the errors were as many as nine. The performance was not necessarily good. In the second match, our country played against Japan, and only three errors were found, but we lost with one to twenty. In the first match between Japan and the Philippines, Japan was defeated with zero runs. The strange skills of the Philippine pitcher caused the Japanese team's batting to fail completely. In the nine innings, Japan only had the opportunity to reach second base three or four times. It can be seen that the Philippine team is strong, and it is difficult for Japan to retain the championship. In the second match between China and the Philippines, the Philippines sent out second-rate characters, and we lost again with fourteen to zero. In the second match between Japan and the Philippines, Japan will probably still lose badly.

Track and Field 230

Our country has made special progress in track and field, but compared with Japan and the Philippines, it is still between a hundred steps and ten steps. If we can score points, our wish has been fulfilled. However, Liu Changchun, who was regarded as the most promising, was eliminated in the preliminary rounds of both short runs, both finishing fourth. Mr. Liu has come to Shanghai several times, but he has never shown his skills. Even in this preliminary track and field selection in our country and the confrontation between China and the West, he did not easily appear. Mr. Liu said that he had a leg injury. Could it be that his leg will never heal? People in the country felt that he was conserving his energy and preparing for the Far Eastern Games to bring glory to the country. But now that he has retired like this, it can be said to be the greatest regret of Mr. Liu's life. No wonder our country's track and field races cannot score points. In the field events, Wu Bixian's high jump of 1.83 meters won fourth place, which was a big surprise. It was not expected by the people of the country, and Mr. Wu himself should also regard it as an unexpected honor. For other events, such as Chen Pao-chiu's shot put, there is only a slim hope, and if Fu Pao-lu's pole vault can get one point, it would also be fortunate.

All-Around 231

Our country is steadily winning the third place in the two relay events, because the Dutch East Indies has players in the pentathlon and decathlon, but no relay team. Wang Chi-huai's pentathlon and Chang Ling-chia's decathlon may have a glimmer of hope.

Swimming 232

Swimming is a specialty of Japan. Although the Philippines has two or three special talents, it is difficult to shake their property. Our country's players are too far apart, and the total defeat is expected. However, the relay swim also counts as points. Our country is steadily in last place (third) and can also get four points. Because Japanese women did not participate in women's swimming, our country's women were able to shine and bring glory to our men.

(6) Mr. Wang's Declaration to Overseas Chinese 233

This time, Cheng-ting led our country's team to the Philippines to attend the Far Eastern Games, and I am very grateful for the warm welcome from all sectors of the overseas Chinese community. This spirit not only shows the overseas Chinese community's love for the motherland, but also encourages the courage of the team. More than 130 members of the team who came to the Philippines were selected from the teams from all over the country. Their strength is stronger than ever before. In various competitions, such as football, basketball, and volleyball, the teams are all domestic elites and are quite confident. As for track and field events, although there is no hope of winning the championship, the results are better than in the previous sessions. All events have teams participating this time, because the purpose of sports is to train a healthy body and cultivate a spirit of cooperation. The championship is secondary. Therefore, even if we know that the competition items have no hope, we will not give up. Our country has made a lot of progress in sports recently, and the government's support is also unwavering. For example, the construction cost of the National Games held in the capital last year reached more than 1.5 million yuan. And Shanghai will also spend more than 1 million yuan to build the most complete venue for the National Games and the 11th Far Eastern Games in four years. In addition, the provinces and regions in the north and south also hold them on time and in different places, because we really want to make the people in all places universally interested in sports and make all cities build complete venues once and for all for the needs of practice. A strong physique is not achieved overnight, and good results must be trained from childhood. European and American powers all excel in sports. Only because they are good at sports can the spirit of cooperation be fully expressed. A strong country must first have a strong race. The education authorities in the country, in view of this, have set training standards for children's sports. There are not a few overseas Chinese here, and I deeply hope that the parents and teachers of overseas Chinese children will also pay attention to it. The Philippine sports authorities have spared no effort in the planning before the meeting and the reception of the team, and all facilities are very complete. I would like to add a few words to express my gratitude.

Central China Games Opened Yesterday Conflict with the Press 238

Staff Member Deng Zezhao's Rude Attitude

All Newspapers Refuse to Publish News

丨Heavy Rain! Postponed Competition丨

(Special dispatch from Hankou, 17th) During the 17th Central China Games, an insult occurred to newspaper reporters. The staff member Deng Zezhao, who was hired by the conference, was a scout cadre of the Provincial Party Department. His attitude was rude and repeatedly embarrassed the press. The entire body of reporters resolved that they could not interview the news of the conference and would absolutely not publish it.

Hankou telegram, the 5th Central China Games was grandly held at the Wuchang Public Sports Ground on the morning of the 16th. At the opening ceremony, the athletes from Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi all lined up to participate. The Honorary President of the Conference, Zhang Xueliang, the Honorary Vice President, Zhang Qun, the President of the Conference, Cheng Qibao, and others all arrived at the venue first. At the time, Zhang Xueliang led all the staff members and the four provincial teams for a week-long parade around the venue. The military band led the way, and the athletes followed. The green grass was like a carpet, and the clear sky was like a curtain, adding a lot to the conference. After the parade, the opening of the conference was announced, the flag was raised, and cannons were fired. The representatives of each team declared, and planes circled in the sky, distributing various leaflets. Then, the chairman, Cheng Qibao, delivered an opening speech, saying that the Central China Games has a history of eleven years, and Hunan, Hubei, Anhui, and Jiangxi have taken turns holding it. However, after the fourth session, it was extended due to the situation. Fortunately, with the support of all parties, this session of the Games can be carried out smoothly, which is very gratifying. Now that the conference has opened today, I deeply hope that all athletes will work hard and bring color to Central China, etc. Next, Zhang Qun, representing Honorary President Chiang Kai-shek, read the training instructions, "A strong physique and full spirit are the mother of all undertakings. The success or failure of an individual's future depends on this, and the rise and fall of the nation's future depends on this. Our country's reputation as the 'Sick Man of Asia,' its long-standing weakness, and its being bullied, and the frequent banditry and severe poisoning in the four provinces of Central China, are the responsibilities of all those who grow up in this country and on this land, and all should regard it as the greatest shame. You students are representatives of the strong and healthy youth of Central China. You gather in one place to learn from each other, and you echo the 10th Far Eastern Games being held in the Philippines, which makes it even more meaningful to learn from each other. I hope that you students will abide by the rules of sports, and further cultivate the morality of propriety, justice, integrity, and shame. Be self-reliant and persevere, and infuse the spirit of sports into your daily life. All actions, including food, clothing, housing, and transportation, must conform to the six major principles of neatness, cleanliness, simplicity, plainness, speed, and certainty. In schools, lead your classmates to revitalize. In society, be the vanguard of transforming the atmosphere. I hope that you will universally develop and accumulate strength, and complete the mission of promoting sports. This is what Zhongzheng most eagerly expects of you students. May you all work hard." Next, Honorary President Zhang Xueliang gave a speech. Honorary Vice President Zhang Qun gave a speech, saying that the four provinces are related in terms of geography, politics, and culture, and suffer the same pain from the spread of banditry. He hoped that they would learn from each other and cooperate thoroughly. Finally, Wang Wei-chun, the representative from Hubei Province, replied on behalf of the athletes, sincerely accepting the instructions from the presidents. After the speech, more than 3,000 Boy Scouts performed group exercises and dispersed. In the afternoon at 2:00 PM, the competition will begin, but due to heavy rain, it could not be held. Cheng Qibao announced that it would be postponed by one day. On this day, the athletes from each province wore homespun clothes and were full of spirit. However, the female athletes from Hubei wore goose-yellow short clothes and green skirts, which had a fairy-like appearance and were the most eye-catching in the entire venue. In terms of technique, each has its own advantages, so it is not yet known who will win. The highest records of the Central China Games in the past are recorded below: Men's Division: (1) Track and Field: 100 meters 12 seconds, 200 meters 25 seconds, 400 meters 57.9 seconds, 800 meters, 2 minutes 15.6 seconds, 1500 meters, 4 minutes 48.6 seconds, 10,000 meters, 37 minutes 46.4 seconds, (2) Field: Shot Put 11.60 meters, Discus 29.04 meters, Javelin 41.01 meters, High Jump, 5.6 feet, Long Jump 5.69 meters, Pole Vault 2.885 meters, Triple Jump 11.83 meters, (3) All-Around: 1600-meter Relay, 3 minutes 56.7 seconds, Pentathlon 2065 points, Decathlon 3570 points, (4) Swimming: 50 meters 35.6 seconds, 100 meters 1 minute 23.6 seconds, 400 meters 8 minutes 17 seconds, 100 meters Backstroke missing, 1500 meters 39 minutes 46 seconds, 200 meters Breaststroke 2 minutes 11.8 seconds, 200-meter Relay 2 minutes 2 minutes 6 seconds. Women's Division: 50 meters 8 seconds, 100 meters 15.4 seconds, High Jump 1.225 meters, Shot Put 7.27 meters, Softball Throw 31.08 meters. The preliminary selections for this session have repeatedly broken records, increasing the 200 meters, javelin, discus, hurdles, 400-meter relay and other events. The future results must be even more impressive.

Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education Will Convene a Meeting of Physical Education Teachers 239

The Meeting is Scheduled for June 5

(Zhenjiang Telegram) In order to improve physical education in secondary schools, the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education has specially convened physical education teachers from various schools to hold a physical education meeting to discuss the implementation of the standards for physical education courses in senior and junior high schools promulgated by the Ministry of Education, as well as the minimum standards for physical education equipment. The meeting is scheduled to open at 3:00 PM on June 5 and will last for three days. Education News

Foreign News: Siam Seals Overseas Chinese Schools 245

Fifteen Overseas Chinese Schools Unjustifiably Closed

Many Chinese Teachers Forced to Leave

| Account of Mr. Huang Chengguan, Teacher at Nanyang Middle School in Siam |

Mr. Huang Chengguan, the Director of Studies at Nanyang Middle School in Siam, has recently returned from Siam. According to Mr. Huang, since the People's Party took power in the Siamese government, there has been a new political atmosphere, and progress has also been made in education. However, there are many overseas Chinese in the area, so the Siamese Ministry of Education has also paid close attention to overseas Chinese education. In recent years, various overseas Chinese schools in Siam, in order to develop overseas Chinese education, have mostly invited teachers from the motherland to teach. Therefore, overseas Chinese education has been flourishing. Unexpectedly, this has aroused the jealousy of the Siamese Ministry of Education. The Siamese believe that the more developed overseas Chinese education is, the more disadvantageous it is to Siamese education. Therefore, the Siamese are constantly trying to prevent the development of overseas Chinese education. For example, last year they implemented compulsory education, forcing overseas Chinese children aged ten to fourteen to study Siamese for 21 hours and 15 minutes per week. This year, they have gone even further, closing as many as 15 overseas Chinese schools for no reason in less than half a month. Not only that, but they have also tried to force Chinese teachers with superior knowledge to resign, such as by setting a deadline for taking the Siamese language exam (stipulating that those who have not taken the Siamese language exam may not become teachers), or by threatening the principals of overseas Chinese schools to force them to resign (the principals of overseas Chinese schools are appointed by the school founders and are elders who know Siamese; the Siamese Ministry of Education legally recognizes only the principals as the owners of the school's rights, so the principals have the power to dismiss Chinese principals and teachers). For example, Mr. Huang Chengguan was forced to return to China by the principal. Mr. Huang had worked in the Normal Department of Huanghun School in Siam. At that time, Siam was implementing compulsory education. Mr. Huang had suggested in various Chinese newspapers that the overseas Chinese should reform education, and he attacked the Siamese compulsory education regulations as unsuitable for overseas Chinese children. Therefore, he aroused the jealousy of the Siamese Ministry of Education and was warned by the Siamese Ministry of Education. Later, the overseas Chinese's opposition to compulsory education failed, and Mr. Huang also left Huanghun School and turned to founding Nanyang Middle School, an overseas Chinese school. However, the Siamese Ministry of Education never forgot about Mr. Huang. Recently, the Siamese Ministry of Education suddenly closed 15 overseas Chinese schools. The Siamese Ministry of Education was deeply afraid that Mr. Huang would rise up again to oppose it. In order to take preemptive action, they threatened the principal of Nanyang Middle School to force Mr. Huang to hand over the administrative power of the school to a Siamese principal, threatening to suspend the school if Mr. Huang did not leave. For the sake of the school, Mr. Huang could not bear to see the school suspended because of him, so he resolutely left the school and returned to China voluntarily. The Siamese Ministry of Education's oppression of various overseas Chinese schools is now in full swing.

100,000 National High School Graduates Enlist in Military Training This Year 247

Enlistment in Beiping, Wuhan, and Nanjing

Female Students Exempt from Military Training

(Special dispatch from Beiping) According to military training officers who came to Beiping from Beijing, the central government has decided to actively reorganize student soldiers. The General Inspectorate of Military Training has reached an agreement with the Ministry of Education that 100,000 graduates from high schools and above nationwide this year must enlist in military training. The training period is three months and does not conflict with their future academic prospects. Graduating students from various provinces in North China will enlist in Beiping, students from Central China will enlist in Wuhan, and students from South China will enlist in Nanjing. Female students from coeducational high schools and girls' middle schools are exempt from military training. Those who voluntarily enlist will be allowed. It is reported that female students from Northeastern University have received military training and many have voluntarily enlisted.

Still not weak, and the various overseas Chinese schools, because they have never been united, are mostly unable to survive. It is hoped that the motherland will provide deep assistance to the overseas Chinese in the area.

Jiangsu Province Actively Preparing for the High School Normal School Joint Examination 248

Scheduled to Begin on the 20th of Next Month

Examination Locations Divided into Nine Districts Throughout the Province

| Examination Questions Will Be Sealed and Opened On the Spot |

(Tongxun from Zhenjiang) The summer graduation joint examination for high schools and normal schools in Jiangsu Province has been scheduled for June 20th to 23rd. It is reported that the entire province has been divided into nine districts. The examination methods and the list of schools in each examination district have been drafted by the Department of Education. The details are recorded separately below.

Examination Methods 249

(1) The examination locations are temporarily divided into nine districts, with Zhenjiang, Wujin, Wuxi, Wuxian, Shanghai, Nantong, Jiangdu, Tongshan, and Nanjing as the examination locations. (2) The examination date is set from June 20th to 23rd, and will be held simultaneously in each district. (3) The chief examiners and supervisors will be appointed by the examination committee in each examination district. The chief examiner will be appointed by the Examination Committee, and the supervisors will be appointed by the Department of Education. (4) Examination Venues: The venues will be borrowed from the examination locations in each district. (5) Seating Arrangement: The seating arrangement for the students taking the examination in each school in each district will follow the principles of mixed distribution and mutual isolation. (6) Examination Questions: The examination questions for each subject will be sealed by the chairman of the committee, stamped with a private seal, and handed over to the chief examiner of each district, who will bring them to be opened on the spot and distributed for use. Each district will use the same examination questions. (7) Examination Papers: The examination papers for each subject will be formulated, numbered, and sealed by the Examination Committee, and after being sealed, they will be handed over to the chief examiner of each district to be opened on the spot and distributed. After the examination is completed and collected, they will still be sealed by the chief examiner, stamped with a private seal, and sent to the committee for grading and scoring, opening the seal, and verifying the names.

List of Examination Schools 250

On the Use of Literary Chinese in Elementary School Textbooks, the Requirement of Reading Mencius in Junior High School, and Various Criticisms of Vernacular Chinese (2) 258

— Wu Yanyin

(6) Mr. Wang said, "One word in literary Chinese conveys the spirit, while dozens of words in vernacular Chinese often fail to express the meaning. Although learning literary Chinese is more difficult, the benefits in the future will surely be many times greater." Education should pay attention to the results, but it should also consider the process. Spending "ten years at the window, only then to understand literary Chinese," can this ten years of effort not be counted in the economic account? Moreover, writing in literary Chinese is mostly incomprehensible, while writing in vernacular Chinese is easy to create. This is also a fact. In the imperial examination era, of those so-called young scholars who specialized in literary Chinese, how many were truly fluent after ten years at the window? Taking Jiangyin as an example, there were many examinees where the "inspector of studies" was stationed, but of the thousands who took the exam, no more than a hundred were truly fluent. The result of reading literary Chinese can be imagined. Mr. Wang has been a middle school principal, and middle schools must emphasize literary Chinese. I ask, among high school graduates, how many out of ten are able to convey the spirit of literary Chinese with one word, and reap the benefits of literary Chinese? The process is very difficult, and the results are not easily good. How can one talk about benefits?

7. Mr. Wang lamented the commodification of textbooks and the use of animal language, which could lead to a disaster like the burning of books. I don't know if commodification or animal language causes the disaster, or if commodification and animal language together cause the disaster. According to Mr. Wang, stories containing allegorical meanings such as "The Mouse Invites Guests" and "The Cat and Dog Hold a Meeting" can be applied to eight-year-old children. Then animal language is not forbidden. If a renowned figure in the education world is able to advocate this view, then the social world can agree. Otherwise, if one does not look at whether the animal language in the textbooks has any allegorical meaning at all, and says "abuse of imagination, without experiencing it," then the so-called "pushing the wave and adding to the billows" is no wonder that outsiders to education deeply resent it blindly. As for the commodification of textbooks, it is difficult to avoid under free competition in buying and selling. If the system is slightly changed, I think the trend can be slightly curbed. Moreover, the commodification of textbooks and the use of animal language are really two separate issues from literary Chinese and vernacular Chinese. Literary Chinese textbooks can also add animal language materials, and they can also be commodified. "Our country's books about gods and ghosts fill many houses." Qian Bao Sou Shen, Strange Tales from a Chinese Studio... are they not all in literary Chinese? Commodified books can really fill five carts. It has been like this for a long time. In the imperial examination era, the grand themes and small themes, and various literary Chinese textbooks before the tenth year of the Republic, were they not all commodified? Taking the classics as an example, Zuo Zhuan has many articles about gods and ghosts, and the Thirteen Classics also have many cases of falsehoods and errors. How can one blame vernacular textbooks alone for animal language and commodification? If vernacular textbooks are enough to start a disaster like the burning of books, then literary Chinese textbooks and all ancient books are enough to start a disaster like the burning of books. I also have an extreme argument: even if the disaster of the burning of books reappears today, there is no need for me to compromise and change vernacular Chinese to literary Chinese. Because if the nature of a book or an argument is wrong, it is not a pity to burn it. If it is right, the blame is not on me. Did Qin Shihuang burn books because the books themselves caused the disaster?

In short, Mr. Wang's argument still seems to be standing on the education world. Although it is slightly biased, it is still the view of one school. Mr. Wang's criticism of vernacular Chinese seems to be outside the education world. Not only are there self-contradictory points, but it also seems to be advocating for "old-fashioned scholars." The attacks of "old-fashioned scholars" outside the education world are not to be feared, but the internal strife within the education world is truly to be feared. Because a renowned figure like Mr. Wang, who has a great reputation in the education world, has actually made this statement, the "old-fashioned scholars" will surely seize it and argue more vigorously. Li Si used the saying of Xun Qing to accomplish Qin Shihuang's perverse acts. Then the disaster of the burning of books was not started by vernacular Chinese, but by Mr. Wang's statement. Does Mr. Wang want to bear this responsibility? I have not expressed my opinion for a long time. I really don't have time to express it, because I value Mr. Wang's statement and cannot help but argue. I did not have time to correct any inappropriate rhetoric. Please forgive Mr. Wang, and please educate the gentlemen of the national education world. (The End)

Spring and Autumn

御香縹緲錄 259

— Original by Princess Der Ling of Qing Dynasty, Translated by Qin Shouou

However, strictly speaking, among the ministers who accompanied the Empress Dowager to Fengtian this time, only Xunling and Qingshan could truly be considered ministers. The rest, frankly, didn't deserve the title. But I think it's only fair to call them accompanying ministers, otherwise it would be unjust. Because I feel that the duties of this group of people are exactly the same, except that when meeting the Empress Dowager, Qingshan and Xunling always stood in the front, there was no other difference. Speaking of standing positions, we have to praise the value of titles. Although I have repeatedly said before that titles are a mere formality and have no practical benefit, when meeting the Empress Dowager, my second brother relied on his title of Duke to always stand in front of Qingshan, even closer to the Empress Dowager. This treatment was considered a great honor at that time. Qingshan was a male housekeeper in the Qing Palace, and he could probably manage everything a male housekeeper could manage. My second brother was like an adjutant to the Empress Dowager, without actual power, but his position was always higher than that of a male housekeeper, so he could stand in front of Qingshan.

Along the way, our train would often be ordered to stop because the Empress Dowager was in a good mood. Whenever the train stopped, Qingshan and Xunling, leading a group of "accompanying ministers," had to come forward to serve her. The Empress Dowager knew almost everyone's names, official titles, and brief personal histories. Although she didn't seem to pay much attention to them when they stood before her, none of their clothes and manners could escape her keen eyes.

"They are all dressed very luxuriously!" she often lamented. "Their extravagance and official airs can indeed add a lot of fun to our journey!" (36)

大肚皮 260

— Qing Qu

Every year I see the Qingming Festival, I always see four executioners, with two pheasant feathers inserted in their heads, wearing red satin jackets and trousers. Those people are all fair-skinned, fat bellied, and swaggering on the road; it is said that they are the owners of meat shops, born to kill pigs from childhood, so they are all famous butchers!

I say big belly, it is not necessary to be an executioner. I often see people sitting in the car, their bodies leaning back, their belly like a bent bow covering them, forming an extreme arc. Isn't this, to put it elegantly, called a fat merchant? Those who have studied know that Wang Xizhi used to be fat bellied, exposing his belly on the eastern bed, and could get a beautiful woman and become a happy son-in-law, how wonderful. Su Dongpo also had a big belly, and every time he finished eating, he had to move slowly. One day, he touched his belly and asked the maid, "What is inside?" Someone replied, "Articles and economics." Only his concubine Chao Yun retorted, "Scholar, you have a belly full of untimely things." Su Dongpo had to hold his belly and laugh. What a romantic affair! Not only these two people, but also when Grand Tutor Dang finished eating, he also pointed to his belly and said, "I will not let you down." His subordinates said, "The general will not let down his belly, this belly will let down the general, and has not contributed much wisdom." Bian Xiaoxian once wanted to sleep during the day, and his disciples mocked him, "Bian Xiaoxian has a big belly, is too lazy to read, and only wants to sleep." Xiaoxian replied, "Bian is my surname, Xiao is my name, big belly, a container for the Five Classics." These two felt that not only their bellies were big, but also their capacity was very large. This is unattainable!

The ancients said: A prime minister's belly is good for rowing a boat. This is also used to describe his generosity, so he can manage the universe, govern the country and secure the people. If we talk about it now: that belly is too small, it really can't hold anything, and there are more knots inside, which makes people unpredictable, making everyone deceive each other, and no one doesn't have their own ideas, causing trouble. What else? The belly is big, hum! Either they are full of money, or they are pregnant, secretly suffering from a ten-month illness, still not as good as the executioner swaggering on the road!

小茶館裹 261

— Rong Yu

The countryside is really lonely! The guys who "work at sunrise and rest at sunset" have nowhere to go except sneak out to a small teahouse during their farming breaks.

What's so fun about a small teahouse? A low, humble house, with a few broken tables and a few long benches. Purple clay teapots and crude porcelain bowls, definitely not brewed with the best tea leaves such as Yuqian or Oolong. But in the morning and evening, a house full of people, the sound of conversations filling the seats, and the smell of cigarettes temporarily change the silent air of the countryside.

The old fathers, with pipes in their mouths and tightly furrowed brows, emit a "singing the past, lamenting the future" tone from their dry throats. The middle-aged uncles inquire about the price of rice and the rise and fall of vegetable prices, as concerned as speculators doing "buying short" and "selling short." The young guys smoke cigarettes and drink strong tea, talking about the scenery of Shanghai. What are the women in Shanghai like? What are the gambling, wine, food, and dramas like in Shanghai? They can't wait to immediately grow wings and fly to Shanghai to experience the prosperous life there.

The old man in the teahouse, while "huffing and puffing" the bellows, fanning the tea stove, is also talking about "Li's aunt in the east village, who is good at having affairs, was caught by her husband last night. Wang Amao in the west lane, who got drunk on spirits, slept on the grave for a night, and today has a severe fever, probably possessed by a wild ghost." He is a "wireless radio" in the countryside; he can also be called a "wordless newspaper," so many people run here, loving to listen to his news.

The countryside is really too lonely! This small teahouse is a lively place in a lonely world.

東北四連長 262

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 28 A Coincidence for Viewing, A Concern for Illness by Handing a Handkerchief, and a Misunderstanding of a Letter

Guizhi, I suddenly understand now that the opportunities of the golden age, although they have been missed, as long as we understand each other, it is not difficult to comfort each other in spirit, right? Okay, I can only write this far. Because I wrote this letter very carefully, so as not to cause any misunderstandings. I wrote and tore, tore and wrote, and have already torn up twenty or so sheets of letter paper. I was also afraid that you wouldn't recognize cursive script, so I wrote in regular script, neatly. Just look at this point, you can know how important I think this letter is. I hope that when you receive this letter, you will read it carefully several times, and then reply to me. It would be even better if we could arrange to meet in person somewhere. I hope this is not too much to ask, right? Wishing you well! Your friend, Gan Jizhi

After writing this letter, Jizhi wrote "To be opened personally by Ms. Yang Guizhi" on the envelope, put it in his inner pocket, and went to bed. When he woke up on the pillow the next day, the first thought that came to his mind was, how should this letter be delivered to Guizhi's hands? Sending it by the post office is definitely inappropriate, because he was afraid that it would fall into the hands of Old Zhao. Let the maid deliver it? That would require at least one more person to participate in this secret. After thinking about it, the only way is to personally deliver it to Guizhi's hands. As for what method to use to personally deliver it to Guizhi's hands, this is not something that can be solved in one day, so he had to wait for an opportunity. He made such a decision, and delayed leaving for two days. He would loiter at the gate several times a day. On the afternoon of the second day, he actually encountered Guizhi coming to the gate. He didn't have time to consider everything else. He bowed from afar, took out the letter, and stretched out his hand to hand it over. When Guizhi saw him handing over the letter, her heart was already pounding wildly. She originally intended not to receive it, but she was afraid that it would be delayed and others would see it, so she had to take the letter, immediately stuff it into her pocket, and her face turned red. (387)

仲良先生自滬寄貽紅梅便面金箋佳筆并況又韓小宋昆仲作書軸印章賦此答謝希眎二況正之 263

— Wang Zhaoming

In the past, I wrote the Ice Spring poem and echoed the words of Huifeng. (Commissioned by Monk Jin Su) In the blink of an eye, forty years have passed. Marquis Qian came south yesterday to discuss the secluded interest of daytime. (You sent me the Red Leaf Pavilion picture and inscription by Huifeng's son and Han) To write the beauty of Lonely Mountain, deep affection entrusted to the brush, carefully selected bristles, fragrant paper that will not be eaten by worms. Also mentioned the virtuous men of Guilin, Dezhu and Wenju. Emerald green sprinkled on pine fat, scarlet carved into flower milk. The secret of Beiyuan is passed down, the method of Xiling can be followed. Suddenly, under the fragrant eaves, strange lights appear like phoenixes and luan. I am ashamed that my humble talent is not up to par, tracing back the lingering sound of cold wild geese. (Huifeng and Jiangcun had a Wild Geese Sound Gathering) I am old in the rivers and lakes, what more can I admire about my humble life? Nostalgia shares the same heart, I cannot bear to leave. A farmhouse remains outside the city (You have a villa in the northern suburbs of Guangzhou), when will I return to travel? Friendship is formed east and west of the mountains, trimming vegetables and getting drunk in the wind and dew.

人物小誌

再書潘蘭史 264

— Lin Yuewei

Mr. Pan Lanshi, with moral integrity and literary talent, was highly respected throughout the country, and lived in seclusion in Shanghai, enjoying himself with poetry and wine. He used to live on North Sichuan Road, Keming Road, and often visited me, talking about poetry and drinking wine, free and unrestrained, often hiring prostitutes to serve wine, listening to songs and dancing, and the excitement was even greater. I once impromptu composed two poems on the spot: "Drunk in the Qionglou night drink, why refuse, there are famous flowers in the seat to illuminate the wine disaster, afraid to listen to Qiu Niang's Golden Thread Song, the green shirt has delayed my youth." "Happy flowers accompany the brocade feast, the fragrance at the bottom of the bracelet floats in the wine cup, the madness of the old Fanchuan has not diminished, and I am happy not to come to the wine." Mr. admired the last sentence very much, chanting it over and over again. I edited the Zhongshe magazine, and Mr. wrote tens of thousands of words of poetry, and there are still manuscripts that have not been published. Since the January 28th Shanghai Incident, Mr. moved to Fuli Road, and meetings became rare. Now that the spring is bright and beautiful, I was planning to visit Mr. and have a good time, but unexpectedly, the bad news came that Mr. had returned to Daoshan, and a wise man had passed away. How can I bear the grief! Therefore, I wrote a couplet to mourn him, saying: "His romantic nature is like Bai Tai Chuan, and his unrestrainedness is comparable to Lu Fangweng. He loves wine and poetry, and lives in seclusion in the lakes and seas for half his life." "His longevity surpasses Rong Qiqi, and his nobility rivals Tao Jingjie. Why envy becoming an immortal or a Buddha? His writings are immortal for thousands of years." I also wrote a couplet on behalf of the Confucian Church, saying: "The holy religion civilizes the barbarians, and lectures in Berlin. You were shocked by your outstanding reputation at a young age, and the commoner could sway the princes and ministers." "Consign emotions to poetry and wine, and hide in Shanghai. It is sighable that his life was bleak, and only his writings remained in his luggage." (No remuneration accepted)

記一位人才 265

— Kouzi

I often hear adults and gentlemen lamenting that "talent is hard to find." Is it really that talent is hard to find? Honestly, in a country and society like this, even if there is real talent, it cannot develop. Therefore, on the one hand, geniuses and extraordinary talents die in obscurity, and on the other hand, everyone clamors that talent is hard to find. It really reminds me of a saying by Han Yu, which is, "Is it really that there are no horses? Is it really that people don't know horses!"

Among the students studying in Japan, I feel awe when I hear that they are students of the Imperial University. Because without a higher school background, one cannot enter the Imperial University. The higher school is like the preparatory course for the Imperial University. The Imperial University does not accept students from outside the higher school in the first year. Therefore, when I hear that someone is a student of the Imperial University, their study qualification is at least five or six years or more. Rarity makes things valuable, which is inevitable.

There is an Imperial University student who has been in Japan for more than ten years. He simply can't think about returning to China. Do you know why? Originally, he was on government funding. As long as he is studying, the country will give him money to use. Moreover, he really has the ability. He can make cosmetics. He makes perfumes, snow creams, hair oils, etc. that are even better than those produced by famous Japanese manufacturers. He drew a trademark himself, registered it with the Japanese government, ordered many glass bottles, printed many advertising papers, and promoted his products to pharmacies in Tokyo. He was unexpectedly welcomed by Japanese women, and the supply almost could not meet the demand. He made a lot of money. A Japanese cosmetic manufacturer wanted to recruit him to be a technician, but he smiled and said, "I make this stuff just to subsidize my tuition. Who wants to help the little devils make money?" So he declined!

This friend and his wife are both in Japan. Basically, the country supplies him with expenses. If the government funding is not enough, he can get some benefits from cosmetics. Wearing a square hat, carefree, truly like a fairy, he enjoys staying here and does not want to return home. Someone advised him to return to China. He said: If I go back to China and want to open my own factory, I don't have the capital. If I want to help others, I'm afraid no one will want me. It's better to be happy and carefree here!

He has made up his mind, so when the graduation deadline arrives, he transfers from the Department of Chemistry to the Department of Pharmacy. After four years, he transfers to the Department of Biology. By switching like this, he becomes an old student of the Imperial University. Once, he talked to me at length about essential oils, and I really admired his erudition. I heard that at the Imperial University, not only Japanese students admire him, but even the professors praise him as extraordinary. But we have been back for six or seven years, and this loving couple is still wandering in a foreign country!

A friend like this must be considered a talent, right? However, he is willing to die in a foreign country. Although his views should not be taken as a lesson, the country and society cannot but bear some responsibility for forcing him onto a deviant path, right?

The gold market yesterday saw a sudden surge in selling pressure due to optimism about the outcome of the silver bill after the meeting between the US President and silver advocates, leading to a sharp drop in market prices and widespread panic. The situation was sluggish, but there was also intense struggle, mainly due to the Guangdong trading houses reversing to buy and the central bank buying spot goods. Initially, the overseas silver markets in the UK and the US all fell, but the closing price of forward silver on the metal exchange actually rose by 0.4 to 1.5 percent. Exchange rates remained stable. London raw gold fell by half a penny, US cotton rose by 6 pounds, and US imports rose by half a point. A telegram from the Associated Press stated that after the meeting between the President and silver advocates, the President and leaders of the silver advocates had agreed on a silver bill in this Congress. The White House also formally announced that the President and silver advocates had reached an agreement. According to the President's opinion, silver legislation to improve the monetary system will be in the form of agency rule. Various silver advocates expressed extreme optimism about the outcome of the meeting. As soon as trading opened, prices fell. Subsequently, it was said that the new silver bill would definitely include recognizing silver as the main currency with a silver reserve of 25%. The Ministry of Finance would have the right to purchase silver at up to $1.29 per ounce. The President would have the power to impose penalties, and silver would be nationalized. It was difficult to stay above the $20 level, and prices gradually fell. Later, Reuters also continuously reported similar news, causing extreme panic. The $10 mark was broken, but there were struggles along the way. Later, due to heavy buying by large traders, the situation improved, and the Guangdong trading houses also came to buy strongly and raise prices. However, the market sentiment was ultimately weak, and there were many declines. At noon, the silver price in the Seattle night market fell by 0.375, rose by 0.125, and then rose by 0.375, stabilizing the situation and hovering. In the aftermarket, the night market silver price opened higher by 0.375, 0.375, and 0.25, but then fell immediately. It was rumored in the market that the US President had requested the power to purchase 1.8 billion ounces of silver, and prices fell again. However, the banks held together, the central bank bought spot goods, and prices were able to rebound. There was news that the Dallas silver bill was revived, and prices fell again, but the domestic market was flat and hovered around $10. Finally, speculator Wu sold, and Bombay rose by seven annas, but the market closed weakly. The price of pure gold was calculated at $1036. The market situation for the day is recorded below.

Silk and Tea; New Silkworms in Jiangsu and Zhejiang Are About to Be Placed on the Shelves 283

Improved Varieties Can Be Expected to Have a Good Harvest

Late Local Silkworms Are Better

Hushu Improved varieties of silkworm eggs in Hushu, Hangzhou, are developing smoothly. The early gang will come out of the fire, and the late gang is also prosperous with leaves. In an instant, they can be placed on the shelves to make cocoons, and a good harvest can be expected. However, there are limited remaining eggs of local varieties left in the area, and the late gang is better.

Xiashi The improved varieties hatched by farmers in the improved silkworm area are entering the big sleep. When the weather turns sunny, the silkworm eggs develop quickly. Some of the early gangs have enough leaves to be placed on the shelves, and the late silkworms only have prosperous leaves. If the weather does not change in the past few days, the silkworm harvest can be expected to be abundant. As for the local silkworms raised in various villages, many have been discarded in the third sleep.

Anji Farmers in the four villages who hatch improved varieties account for 60%. Local varieties are mostly from Zhuji and Yuhang. Due to bad weather, there has been quite a lot of damage in the second sleep. The improved variety of silkworms has been turned from danger to safety by the instructors who have adjusted the temperature and humidity. Now that the weather is warm and the ants have passed well, the early gang has opened the leaves in the third sleep, and the current situation is quite good.

Yangzhong The local silkworms raised by farmers in various cities and villages have been greatly affected by the adverse weather conditions in the second sleep, and many have died stiffly. The development of improved varieties is delayed. After the new mulberry is chopped and the silkworms are fed, the loss is still small. Fortunately, the weather has turned sunny and warm, and the development has turned around. The early gang has been sleeping for three days, and the leaf eating is gradually prosperous. The local silkworms have also passed well.

Japan Japan's silkworm season is earlier than that of our country. Now Wei Nong's automatic limit on the production of spring cocoons, the number of ants raised is reduced, and the weather is bad. Although silkworm farmers pay attention to scientific breeding, the weather is unfavorable and slightly affected. The spring cocoons have already seen the new, and it is expected that the national cocoon production will be reduced by 25% compared with last year, and the cocoon quality is still excellent.

White Factory Warp and Weft New Goods Have Been Thrown Open 284

The New York silk weaving factory has canceled the saying that it will stop work for a week because the sales of silk are gradually turning around. Raw silk factories are gradually rising, and importers have telegraphed to various foreign firms in this port to inquire about market prices. The European firms have also taken advantage of the cheap prices to throw and buy new futures silk, so the white factory warp and weft new futures goods for July and August have been thrown open. It is estimated that Dachang and others have entered 130 bales of upper middle body, and the price is still firm.

Suian Zhenmei Has Been Launched 285

New Suian Zhenmei green tea from the road has arrived in Shanghai. Yesterday, Xie Lihua Tea and other firms opened the first dish at 120-122 yuan, which is about 4-5 yuan lower than last year. However, since this market has been launched, the demand from various firms has been quite strong. It is expected that the later new goods will not be very sluggish. The market for local Zhuang Zhenmei green tea has slightly declined, but the going is not very lonely. Yesterday, the market Xiehe, Jinlong, Tianyu and other firms have all entered. Wenzhou black tea continues to sell well, and the price is firm. Only the Wenzhou Zhenmei item, the going is slightly sluggish.

Yesterday, the sugar market saw a slight recovery in customs gold, with a softening trend. The guild's listed price for Grade 14 coarse granulated white sugar was $20.90, down 8 cents, with few transactions. Re-export goods were traded at $6.77, down 3 cents. This has created a disparity compared to the local price, with a difference of as much as half a dollar.
